[\[1b.1\]{D1853}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_dwakra ma tat+t+wa b+hA wan nA ma mu khA ga ma/_bod skad du/_rim pa gnyis pa'i de kho na nyid bsgom pa zhes bya ba'i zhal gyi lung /_thams cad mkhyen pa
[\[1b.2\]]la phyag 'tshal lo/_/dpal ldan bde rdzogs zab gsal gnyis med 'od zer ldan/_/de yi rang bzhin zhi ba bcu drug phyed cha 'bar/_/don dam snying po de ston bla ma gsum po rab/_/de la bya byed
[\[1b.3\]]gsum mnyam pa yis rtag tu 'dud/_/'jig rten gsum gyi sgron ma kun gyis rab bsngags pa/_/chos rnams kun gyi snying po dngos po'i de bzhin nyid/_/srid pa'i dug chu zlog byed gsum khong waM
[\[1b.4\]]steng 'bar/_/'jam dbyangs bla ma'i lung gis rtogs phyir bshad par bya/_/dbus kyi yul chen kha bir grong khyer rdo 'jog tu/_/bzang po seng ge zhes byar grags pa rab thob pa/_/bla ma de ni mnyes byas
[\[1b.5\]]lung thob gzhung mang thos/_/de la rnam dpyad rig 'byung shI len na len+d+rar/_/yon tan bshes gnyen zhes bya rigs can de yi ngor/_/blun blos rab tu byed pa phyogs 'ga' rtsom byed pa'i/_/brod
[\[2a\]]
[\[2a.1\]]pas der gnas rnams la gzhung des phan gdags par/_/bsams nas der gnas rtsom dang ston sogs rab tu byas/_/de nas yon tan kun 'byung u rgyan yul du bgrod/_/'jo sgeg rdo rje zhes byar mtshan
[\[2a.2\]]gsol rab tu grags/_/de la mang thos rnam par dpyad cing de nyid du/_/gu ne nu grags bla ma de yang mnyes byas te/_/lung thob gnas de'i byang phyogs chab sgo bdag_/dzA thig dza la zhes bya'i bu mo bcu drug pa/_/lak+Sh+mI chen
[\[2a.3\]]mo mnyes byas zla ba brgyad kyi bar/_/de yi lung ni rab thob mnos nas grub pa thob/_/de nas dzAlen+d+ha rar grong khyer ko no dzer/_/phyin nas bA li pA da zhes byar grags pa rab thob gang /_/mnyes byas gzhung thos lung ni
[\[2a.4\]]mang du thos gyur nas/_/lho phyogs nam mkha'i shing ldan kong ka na ru bgrod/_/grub pa'i dbang phyug bA li pA dar rab grags pa/_/rdzu 'phrul ldan pa'i slob ma'i tshogs dang rab tu bcas/_/de kun yo byad gos zas nor rgyun
[\[2a.5\]]gyis sbyor ba/_/bla ma dam pa de drung lo dgu rab tu btud/_/'dus pa'i rgyud chen 'grel bcas bco brgyad rab tu mnyan/_/bdag gis ma rtogs bla ma chen pos de bzhin gsungs/_/'dir ma rtogs par gzhan ni don med par
[\[2b\]]
[\[2b.1\]]bsams nas/_/glegs bam mgul btags byang phyogs yul du rab bgrod de/_/rdo rje gdan rgyab ku ba rtsa zhes bya ba'i tshal/_/stag dang dred sogs mang zhing shin tu 'jigs pa'i sar/_/zla ba drug gnas pa yis chos rnams de nyid rtogs/_/sprul pa'i dge slong bla ma gnyis dang bcas
[\[2b.2\]]dang phrad/_/mgo dang lag gnyis yol dang tshes brgyad rgyal la bab/_/ston zla ra ba'i tho rangs skya rengs shar dus su/_/'jam dpal dbyangs kyis dkyil 'khor 'khor lor sprul pa la/_/bdag gis don 'di blang phyir gsol ba rab tu btab/_/khyod ni sems can kun gyi yab ste
[\[2b.3\]]yum yang yin/_/khyod kyis bdag la sogs te 'jigs pa che las skyobs/_/'gro ba'i dbang po rje btsun khyod kyis sdug bsngal sel/_/khams gsum stong byed chi ba che khyod skye bo skyongs/_/thog ma med khyod nga ro thigs pa'i steng cha med/_/rje btsun yid med bdud rtsi rab dga'
[\[2b.4\]]bde btang byed/_/'gro la phan phyir bde bas sangs rgyas rnams kun la/_/rab dgyes bde ba'i mgon chen khyod kyis gtang bar mdzod/_/skyon gyis ma gos bla na med pa'i byang chub lam/_/sna tshogs sdug bsngal zhi mdzad skom pa ngoms mdzad cing /_/'khor ba dba' klong thar mdzad
[\[2b.5\]]bde la 'god mdzad pa/_/dngos kun rgyal bas mi dpogs lam 'di bstan par mdzod/_/zhi ba'i zhi ba rdul dang rab bral 'dzum pa spangs/_/bsgom pa las 'das mkha' 'dra dri mas ma gos pa/_/sgyu ma kun 'das 'dod pa kun la rgyab kyis phyogs/_/de 'dra'i rje btsun khyod la bdag
[\[2b.6\]]ni skyabs su mchi/_/dregs med 'jigs med byang chub chen po thob kyi bar/_/'khor bar 'tsho bar 'jig rten dmyal rtsub ma lhung bar/_/khyod gsung dam tshig sdom pa thun mong ma yin rnams/_/bdag la sogs pas rtag tu rab tu bskyang bar bgyi/_/gar chen rnam par rol pas gar mdzad
[\[2b.7\]]cing /_/sna tshogs phyag ni bcu dang bsgyings pa yis/_/pad+mo lo ma 'jam pa brgyad phye nas/_/gnyis med bde rgyu rdo rje gzhag par mdzod/_/gsang ba'i de nyid mi nyams gsal bar 'gyur/_/rdo rje 'dab skyes zla ba'i yang dag 'du/_/thabs shes las byung chos kun de nyid mchog_/rje btsun
[\[3a\]]
[\[3a.1\]]bdag la phan phyir sbas pa shod/_/de nas 'jam dbyangs byang chub sems dpa' chen po yis/_/bdag la 'dzum pa'i bzhin bltas legs zhes lan gsum gsungs/_/rol pa'i gar dang chos kun de bzhin nyid/_/sgra brnyan lta bur rdo rje glu yis bdag
[\[3a.2\]]la bstan/_/a bi yaM raM baM laM hUM a la la ho/_/rje btsun thugs rje che rnams kyis/_/'di rtogs pa yis bde gshegs kyi/_/phun sum tshogs pa 'thob 'gyur ba'i/_/'das dang da ltar ma byon pa'i/_/rdo rje 'dzin pas snod 'ga' la/_/gsungs shing gsung dang gsung 'gyur
[\[3a.3\]]ba/_/yang dag don rab rab rtogs phyir/_/nga yis khyod la bstan par bya/_/yid gcig bsdus la mnyan par gyis/_/chos rnams gzugs la sogs pa rnams/_/kun mkhyen bar gyi rang bzhin ni/_/nam mkha'i dkyil ltar rnam dag pa'i/_/zab gsal gnyis med ye shes
[\[3a.4\]]te/_/de ni dngos med bsgom dngos med/_/dngos po thams cad dang bral ba'i/_/khams dang skye mched kyis ma zin/_/rang bzhin gyis ni 'od gsal ba/_/gdod nas dag pa nam mkha' bzhin/_/med nas chos rnams mtshan nyid spangs/_/chos dang chos nyid yang med de/_/dngos
[\[3a.5\]]po med pas mkha' dang mtshungs/_/tshig dang yi ge kun las grol/_/de ni dus dang phyogs rnams dang /_/chos kun gyi ni ngo bor song /_/lus ma yin te ngag dang ni/_/yid kyang ma yin 'dod khams dang /_/gzugs dang gzugs med khams ma yin/_/'byung chen bzhi yang ma
[\[3a.6\]]yin te/_/de bas de ni gang na yang /_/mi gnas pas na mnyam pa nyid/_/de 'dra rdo rje 'chang chen po/_/chos rnams kun gyi chos nyid mchog_/thabs kyis bsgrub par bya ba'i dngos/_/brtag pa kun las rab dben pa/_/phun sum tshogs rgyu dpag dka' ba/_/phyag rgya chen por rab
[\[3a.7\]]snang ba'i/_/zer gyis rang gzhan smin byed pa'i/_/de gnyis med pa'i rang bzhin mchog_/rdo rje 'dzin pa chen pos kyang /_/brjod du med pa'i sku chen po/_/de nyid rgyal sras zhing bcas dang /_/srid gsum rgyu dang mi rgyur bcas/_/thams cad kun gyi bdag nyid de/_/dngos kun gtso bo
[\[3b\]]
[\[3b.1\]]rang sems kyi/_/ngo bo nyid de de rtogs na/_/sangs rgyas byang chub de nyid do/_/'jig rten gsum yang de nyid do/_/'byung chen rnams kyang de nyid do/_/ci yi phyir na chos thams cad/_/sems la gnas te de nyid kyang /_/nam mkha' la gnas nam mkha' ni/_/gang du mi gnas 'od
[\[3b.2\]]gsal ba/_/gzod nas rnam dag stong pa'o/_/sangs rgyas mya ngan 'das pa'i khams/_/skye med rdo rje mngon byang chub/_/bder gshegs kun gyi snying po mchog_/gnyis med rtog bral don chen te/_/rim pa gnyis par rab tu bshad/_/de 'dra'i don des dngos po kun/_/rnam par
[\[3b.3\]]khyab ste rnam gnas kyang /_/thog med dus nas de las kyang /_/rnam rtog chen po tshul byung ste/_/de las yang ni 'byung ba che/_/rlung gi dkyil 'khor nyid byung ste/_/de las kyang ni me yi khams/_/chen po byung nas khyab mdzad de/_/de las chu khams chen po yang /_/byung ste khyab mdzad
[\[3b.4\]]de las kyang /_/sa byung bzhi bsdus ngo bo las/_/ri sogs sems can thams cad kyang /_/sna tshogs phra ba sbom po dang /_/skyes pa bud med ma ning dang /_/gzhon nu dang ni rgan po dang /_/lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang /_/gdon dang skar ma gshin rje dang /_/chu bdag brgya byin dmyal
[\[3b.5\]]ba dang /_/yi dgas dud 'gro dang de kun/_/spangs dang shes tsam rab brten pa'i/_/'gro ba kun du rgyas par gnas/_/de bas de yi gong ma yi/_/gnyis med rtog bral rab bsgrims te/_/ma rtogs pas na 'gro ba kun/_/'khor bar rab tu 'khor bar 'gyur/_/de ni 'khor ba'i
[\[3b.6\]]sdug bsngal che/_/dug chu lta bur 'khrul pa yis/_/rnam bsgrubs thag pa'i sbrul lta bur/_/snang zhing med pa nyid du 'dod/_/de bas gnyis med don chen po/_/rang rig dkyil 'khor chen po mchog_/rgyun dang rnam grangs kyis gnas pas/_/de yi ngo bo rtogs par bya/_/gang zhig
[\[3b.7\]]de rtogs rab 'dun pa/_/sems kyi smon lam yang dag can/_/sngon du bsod nams mthu bskyed dang /_/skyes bu yang dag bzhi la brten/_/spro dang gus dang bsnyen bkur dang /_/'dun par ldan zhing sgom pa dang /_/brtan po som nyi rnam spangs pa/_/rjes mthun gtong phod des shes 'gyur/_
[\[4a\]]
[\[4a.1\]]de yis rje btsun yang dag pa/_/mchog gi gdams ngag rgyud la ldan/_/theg chen lam gyi spyod pa dang /_/bsgom pa la ni lhur len dang /_/de nyid bcu la sogs pa yi/_/gsang dang rab gsang shin tu gsang /_/shes shing de yi don gab par/_/ston byed bla ma
[\[4a.2\]]mnyes par bya/_/yul dang mkhar dang khyim dang rta/_/glang po che sogs mal stan dang /_/chung ma sdug dang yid 'ong bu/_/bu mo sring mo tsha mo sogs/_/gzhan yang gser dang dngul gyi rdzas/_/zangs lcags sogs las byas pa yis/_/mdzes pa'i rdzas dang mu tig gi/_/phreng dang pad+ma
[\[4a.3\]]rA ga dang /_/pu shar in+d+ra nI la dang /_/margad g.yu sogs mchod pa'i tshogs/_/zhing 'di mkhas pas rab bkang ste/_/de 'dra'i rje btsun dbang po mchod/_/gsal zhing rab dga' mkha' mnyam pa/_/gzhan du rigs par mi 'gyur bas/_/bud med sgyu ma'i phyag rgya ni/_/sgyu ma kun las
[\[4a.4\]]khyad par 'phags/_/sgyu ma de yang 'jig rten 'dir/_/spyan la sogs par rnam dag par/_/rigs ni rnam pa bzhir 'gyur te/_/ming dang mtshan nyid bshad par bya/_/ka ma lI dang shad+khI ni/_/tsi tri ni dang ha stI ni/_/dang po klu mo'i rigs yin te/_/gnyis pa stag dang seng ge'i rigs/_/gsum
[\[4a.5\]]pa ri dgas kr-iSh+Na sogs/_/bzhi pa glang po che rigs so/_/de la ka ma lI yi ni/_/dbyibs dang mtshan nyid bstan par bya/_/bu mo pad+ma'i dri bro zhing /_/ngo zlum sna rtse til 'dra ste/_/sen mo dmar zhing rgyab sgur dang /_/rkang mthil kun gyis sa la reg_/ba spu 'khyil ldan sen mo can/_/dkar
[\[4a.6\]]'chang til gyi 'bras bu 'dra/_/gsus pa gnyer ma gsum ldan zhing /_/brang mdzes glang chen ltar 'gros dang /_/rak+ta'i ro ni skar ba'o/_/sha mdog dmar te lha mo 'di/_/mA ma kI yis rnam par dag_/shad+khI ni yi mtshan nyid dang /_/dbyibs ni khyod la bstan par bya/_/bu mo ba tsha'i dri
[\[4a.7\]]bro zhing /_/skra ni ring zhing sna yang ring /_/dkar 'chang na ra ga 'dra ba/_/'o ma zho la rab tu sred/_/rak+ta'i ro ni mngar ba'o/_/mdog ni dkar ser gnas pa yi/_/gos dkar mo yis rnam par dag_/de bzhin tsi tri na ya ni/_/dbyibs dang mtshan nyid bshad par bya/_/bu mo sha rlon dri bro
[\[4b\]]
[\[4b.1\]]zhing /_/lus chung brla ni shin tu mdzes/_/dkar 'chang shing thog pa la 'dra/_/ngo tsha med cing khro 'dod pa/_/rtag tu 'thab mo dag la dga'/_/rje ngar bya rog rkang 'dra zhing /_/mchu 'phyang gan rkyal du nyal ba/_/phug ron skad 'dra sha mdog ni/_/sngo bsangs rak+ta'i ro tsha ba'o/_/de ni lha
[\[4b.2\]]mo sgrol mas dag_/ha stI ni yi mtshan nyid dang /_/dbyibs ni nga yis bstan par bya/_/bu mo chang gi dri bro zhing /_/byin sbom sna ni cung zad yo/_/dri nga zhing ni lus sbom dang /_/spyod pa rtsing zhing mdog rdul skya/_/dkar 'chang g.yas g.yon du dgye ba/_/sha mdog smug cing rak+ta'i ro/_/bsngal
[\[4b.3\]]zhing de 'dra'i bu mo ni/_/sangs rgyas spyan mas dag pa'o/_/da ni de dag thams cad kyi/_/rung dang mi rung spyod pa bstan/_/rol tshe rgyab kyis phyogs pa dang /_/khong du dga' zhing tshig mang dang /_/bsgo ba bzhin du bka' yang gcog_/'o byas kha ni 'phyi byed de/_/bla ma'i yon tan shes
[\[4b.4\]]'gyur yang /_/gzhan du de la cung zad bsnyad/_/bla ma ma mthong ltar byed cing /_/'ongs kyang de la phyag mi 'tshal/_/rje btsun de dang mi mthun pa'i/_/mi gzhan dang ni rtse dga' byed/_/de sogs rab tu mi rung ste/_/mkhas pas rab tu spang bar bya/_/rung ba 'di ni mkhas pas
[\[4b.5\]]btsal/_/mig gi rtsa mdangs mig rtsa rgod/_/sla zhing skad cig bsam pa dang /_/skad cig rgod pa'i 'phro bzhag nas/_/bsam zhing yang na smra'am 'dzum/_/rje btsun bla ma mthong gyur na/_/dga' zhing mdzes lta 'dzum par byed/_/de yi bka' stsal nyan zhing mos/_/steg pa'i tshul
[\[4b.6\]]gyis zhe sar ldan/_/gzhan du de la snyan par brjod/_/de mthong 'grogs la 'khyud cing bsnyen/_/phag tu 'khri zhing sor tshigs nyed/_/skra ni bkrol nas slar 'ching byed/_/gos 'chos shing ni bar bar 'dzum/_/bla ma ma mthong ltar byed cing /_/gos 'chos pa dang lus nyed dang /_/rkang pas sa la
[\[4b.7\]]'drud cing 'dri/_/bus pa'i kha la 'o byed cing /_/nu ma ston cing ske rags 'grol/_/rje btsun de yis ma mthong na/_/glu dbyangs len cing mthong bar byed/_/de ni gang la gnas pa der/_/don med bsnyad kyis 'gro ba dang /_/drag tu gad mos rab steg ste/_/lu zhing glal ba ltar byed cing /_/
[\[5a\]]
[\[5a.1\]]mi mo 'di yang sten par byed/_/da ni gsang gnas dbyibs kyi ni/_/mtshan nyid rung dang mi rung ba/_/nga yis yang dag bstan par bya/_/yid gcig bsdus la mnyan par gyis/_/gyo mo lta bu kha sbub dang /_/khung ring shin tu mi sdug dang /_/rtag tu skam por
[\[5a.2\]]gnas pa dang /_/rtag tu zil pa 'dzag pa dang /_/sbal pa'i rgyab ltar rtsub pa yi/_/gnas ni spang bya mi rung ngo /_/rus sbal rgyab ltar 'phang mtho zhing /_/steng mnyam shin tu 'jam po dang /_/ba glang gi ni ltag pa ltar/_/steng mnyam thog gi dbyibs kyang ring /_/pad+ma'i snying po bzhin
[\[5a.3\]]du zlum/_/cung zhig 'dzag min cung zad 'byung /_/sbu nyung sgyu ma'i phyag rgya ni/_/mkhas pas thabs kyis shin tu btsal/_/mtshan nyid de dang mi ldan yang /_/rigs dang gzugs dang lang tshor ldan/_/rgyan mdzes yid 'ong bu mo ni/_/longs spyod gsum ldan gzung bar bya/_/
[\[5a.4\]]chos zab la mos sems dang ni/_/las 'brel gyis 'khyud ma byas dang /_/sngon gsungs grogs kyis shes bslus pa'i/_/mi mo yang ni mkhas pas bsgrubs/_/de ltar de sogs bud med kyi/_/sgyu ma'i phyag rgya chen pos ni/_/'jig rten gsum du rnyed dka' ba'i/_/lhag pa'i
[\[5a.5\]]lha zhes bya ba sgrub/_/de yang thun mong dang bcas pa/_/tshogs kyi mchod pa yang byas te/_/gang gsungs bu mo btsal nas kyang /_/bla ma la ni dbul bar bya/_/de nas bla ma de mnyes nas/_/de dang snyoms par zhugs pa yis/_/bde gshegs zhu gyur bcu drug char/_/gyur pa slob
[\[5a.6\]]ma'i kha ru ltung /_/ltung bas snying gi pad+mar zhugs/_/de yis zhing ni dag byas te/_/chos kun sgyu ma la sogs pa'i/_/bcu gnyis don du rtogs par 'gyur/_/de nas de la rang 'byung gi/_/chos sku rab dga' mkha' mnyam pa/_/lhag pa'i lha zhes bya ba ni/_/rtogs bya'i
[\[5a.7\]]ched du bu mo byin/_/lha mo 'di ni khyod dang mthun/_/sems can khyod kyis 'dod pa gyis/_/yid 'ong bu mo 'di nyid ni/_/sangs rgyas kun gyis spyod du gnang /_/dkyil 'khor 'khor lo'i cho ga yis/_/bu mo sgrol byed dga' byin ma/_/byang chub chen po bsgrub pa'i phyir/_/khyod_
[\[5b\]]
[\[5b.1\]]kyis bde chen myong bar gyis/_/gzhan gyis sangs rgyas mi nus pa/_/bu mo 'di ni yang dag mchog_/de bas mtha' med 'khor ba'i bar/_/khyod kyis 'di dang bral mi bya/_/de nas sems can de yis ni/_/yid 'ong bu mo blangs byas te/_/de yis dam tshig sdom pa'i mchog_/_
[\[5b.2\]]tshig 'dis rab tu smra bar bya/_/smros shig bu khyod rdo rje can/_/sha khrag khu ba la sogs pa/_/dri chen dri chu sogs za'am/_/b+ha ga 'o byed mi rtog gam/_/gzungs mang la khyod brod dam/_/de yis bzhad gad dang ldan par/_/kye lha mo ci phyir bdag mi brod/_/dri chen dri chu sogs
[\[5b.3\]]za'o/_/lha mo khyod la bkur sti dgos/_/b+ha ga 'o byed nga mi rtog_/de nas bu mos ga sha phud/_/pad+ma gsal bstan tshig 'dis bstod/_/e ma ho bdag gi pad+ma 'di/_/bde ba thams cad dang ldan pa/_/cho ga'i rim pa gang gis spyad/_/de yi mdun na rtag tu gnas/_/don
[\[5b.4\]]byed pad+ma dam pa 'di/_/sangs rgyas kun gyis bkur ba'i gnas/_/rang 'byung bde ba chen po ni/_/'di na rtag par bzhugs pa yin/_/b+hany+dza mok+Sha ho/_/de nas rang gi sa bon las/_/'od zer stug pos nang gsal nas/_/lha yi 'khor lo chags byas nas/_/rdo rje nang
[\[5b.5\]]nas phying byung ste/_/pad+ma'i nang du zhugs byas nas/_/rig ma'i lha yi 'khor lo rnams/_/chags pa chen po bskyed nas kyang /_/zhal nas zhal zhugs 'khor lo rnams/_/chags chen bskyed nas rdo rjer phyung /_/sngon bzhin zhugs sogs rab byas pas/_/yang nas yang du
[\[5b.6\]]lha'i dkyil 'khor/_/yid kyis shin tu chags par bya/_/de nas 'dod pa'i sgyu ma'i tshig_/brjod pas bu mo chags par bya/_/gnyis su med pa bde ba chen po mchog_/lha mo khyod ni sgyu ma'i phyag rgya ste/_/zhal bzang khyod ni nga dang lhan cig tu/_/rnam par brtson pas mkha'
[\[5b.7\]]'dra myang bar bya/_/des kyang sgyu ma lta bu yi/_/'dod pa'i tshig gis gsol btab nas/_/bdag nyid chags pa chen po yang /_/bskyed nas rtsa yi 'khor lo btsal/_/bde mchog rgya chen bdag la dgongs su gsol/_/bsam mi khyab pa'i bde chen dag dang ldan/_/mi g.yo
[\[6a\]]
[\[6a.1\]]tshig dang bral ba'i dbyangs snyan pas/_/bdag la khyod kyis rol cig bzhengs su gsol/_/ngo mtshar che ba'i rol pas snang mdzad cing /_/byang chub snying por 'gro ba'i lam mchog 'di/_/rgyud rnams yang dag gang la mi rten pas/_/bde chen yid 'ong
[\[6a.2\]]nga yis grol bar gyis/_/ho ho ho/_/rol cig rol cig bdag la rol/_/'dod pa gyis shig dga' gsol ba/_/khyod kyis gzhan du mi rtogs pa/_/rtogs pas the tshom ma byed cig_/a la la ho/_/de nas rab tu chags ldan pas/_/de dang lhan cig lus kyi ni/_/spyod
[\[6a.3\]]pas dben pa'i gnas su spyad/_/rol pas dga' ba brtag par bya/_/dang por 'dus pa byas nas su/_/de nas gru mo mtshan nyid dang /_/yang ni brkyang par bya ba dang /_/de bzhin yar bteg mtshan nyid dang /_/shin tu brkyang pas lnga ru 'gyur/_/dpung pa rab tu brkyang byas nas/_/
[\[6a.4\]]gru mo mdud pas mgul nas 'khyud/_/bcing bas dam 'khyud g.yas g.yon skra/_/mgo ni mi g.yo bzung nas blta/_/de nas brla gnyis bar bltas te/_/bung ba lta bu zid sgra'i glu/_/blangs nas mchu yis rtse bar bya/_/'gying bag stabs kyis 'khyud nas ni/_/g.yon gyis
[\[6a.5\]]spyi bo'i skra bzung ste/_/g.yas kyis lkog ma brten nas kyang /_/ma mchu'i sbrang rtsi gzhib par bya/_/gzhib cing zid sgra brjod nas kyang /_/nu ma lag rtsa mgrin pa dang /_/ma mchu 'gram pa rna ba'i rtsa/_/mig dang spyi bo gsang bar yang /_/kha yis 'o byas rtse bar bya/_/rna ba gnyis
[\[6a.6\]]dang mchan khung dang /_/mgrin pa gnyis dang sum mdo rnams/_/sen mo re mos gdab par bya/_/nu ma gnyis dang mchan khung gnyis/_/gtso gnyis dang ni 'gram pa gnyis/_/lag mthil gnyis dang rkang mthil gnyis/_/mnyes pas mdza' ba chen po 'grub/_/g.yon
[\[6a.7\]]gyis pad+ma'i dkyil 'khor ni/_/mnye zhing lce yis bskyod par bya/_/steng 'og tu yang blta byas nas/_/sems kyis de la chags par bya/_/de nas dga' ba'i bu mo des/_/pad+ma bstan nas 'di skad smra/_/rang byung bde chen rgyal po ni/_/pad+ma 'di la rab tu gnas/_/rtsa dang rlung
[\[6b\]]
[\[6b.1\]]gis rtogs 'gyur bas/_/khyod kyi rtsa yi 'khor lo tshol/_/de nas de yi sor mo yis/_/nang nas rtsa yi 'khor lo che/_/pad+ma la gnas snying po lngas/_/rgyan byas ze'u 'bru ge sar dang /_/'dab ma brgyad pa gsal byas nas/_/A li kA li man+t+ra dang /_/kur ma ka dang sha sha ka_/nA
[\[6b.2\]]li gsum po btsal bar bya/_/rdo rje dbyings kyi dbang phyug rtsa/_/gzung 'dzin bral ba b+ha ga'i dbus/_/bla ma'i man ngag stobs kyis ni/_/sor mos go bar bya dgos so/_/de nas sa bcu dang ldan pa'i/_/lha mo de la 'khyud par bya/_/rdo rje pad+mar reg pa ni/_/bsnyen pa'i de nyid
[\[6b.3\]]yin par bshad/_/rdo rje pad+mar zhugs pa ni/_/nye bar sgrub pa'i de nyid do/_/de nas bsgul zhing bskyod tsam gyis/_/snying ni 'dar zhing dran pa nyams/_/spyi bo'i skra grol gos kyang 'dor/_/rdul gyis lus khyab mdog dmar te/_/mig dmar phra bas bdag la blta/_/yang du bskul
[\[6b.4\]]bas bsgrub pa'o/_/de bas sems khral med pa ru/_/sdom brtson gzhu dbyibs g.yo ba yis/_/sum mdo ye shes me sbar nas/_/khams bzhus nas ni bcu drug char/_/gyur pa me tog kun+da 'dra/_/rlung gi sbyor bas phul bar bya/_/rang bzhin gyis ni rab zhi ba/_/chos kun zhi ba de kho
[\[6b.5\]]na/_/bde ba de nyid nor bur 'dug_/skad cig dran med g.yo bar byed/_/sgrub pa chen po de nyid do/_/nam mkha'i khams dang rdo rje sbyor ba las ni yang dag spyan can bde chen 'byung bar 'gyur/_/gang gang yang dag dga' byed chags bral dga' gnyis bar du bden gnyis mthong
[\[6b.6\]]byas brtan par gyis/_/pad+ma'i mkha' la rdo rje nor bu pad snying gnyis la 'byor dang rdo rje skyil krung sems/_/nor bu'i bar du mthong byas gang de bde ba 'byung ba nges par de nyid ye shes te/_/'di ni rdzogs pa'i rim pa yin par bla ma mchog rnams kun gyis yang dag bshad/_/'dod chags

[\[7a\]]
[\[7a.1\]]thams cad kyi/_/mtha' yi de nyid zab gsal ba/_/thog med dus nas so so yi/_/skye bo nga dang ngar 'dzin pas/_/ma brtags par ni bdag tu bzung /_/dus las byung dang 'dod rgyal dang /_/gnam gyis bskos dang gyin dang /_/'dzin pa pos ni sprul pa dang /_/

[\[7b\]]
[\[7b.1\]]yang dag min pas bla dang bcas/_/'og ma 'og ma'i rnal 'byor blo/_/gong ma gong ma'i khyad par 'phags/_/'og ma'i blo ni gong ma yi/_/shes rab kyis ni sun 'byin no/_/de bas gong ma'i rim pa yis/_/lhan cig pa yi slob dpon gyis/_/byin gyis brlabs pa yang dag bya/_/

[\[9b.1\]]'gyur/_/de yang bzung ba goms pa yis/_/phyin ci log ni rnam par ldog_/smig rgyu lta bu snang ba ni/_/rtags ni dang por shes par bya/_/de bzhin du ni chu log pas/_/du ba lta bur 'byung ba ni/_/gnyis pa yin par shes par bya/_/me ni rnam par log gyur pas/_/mkha' snang

[\[11a\]]
[\[11a.1\]]ji ltar bzlas pa byed/_/de bas glang chen rnyed gyur pa/_/rjes kyis de la ci zhig bya/_/don de la gnas rnal 'byor che/_/phyi rol yang ni rten mi 'gal/_/glang po che yi stobs kyis ni/_/bud shing 'byung ba lta bu'o/_/de bas rdo rje bzlas pa mchog_/'bad
[\[11a.2\]]pas bde gshegs thams cad kyi/_/byin brlabs nyid ni 'ong bas na/_/phyag rgya chen po 'grub pa yi/_/mtshan ma yang dang yang 'byung 'gyur/_/de 'byung cho ga la gnas pas/_/skad cig gis ni kun mkhyen che/_/rgyud las rab tu 'pho bar ni/_/the tshom med par
[\[11a.3\]]nges pas na/_/cho ga 'di la rab tu 'bad/_/de ltar dga' gsum bye brag gi/_/thig le rnam gsum bsgom pa yi/_/cho ga yang dag bstan pa'o/_/da ni gnyis med ye shes nyid/_/kun rdzob gzugs la brten nas kyang /_/mi g.yo la sogs g.yo dang bcas/_/tshangs
[\[11a.4\]]sogs lha dang lha min sogs/_/thams cad rab tu mi snang yang /_/thig le 'gog par mi 'gyur te/_/rgyu dang mi rgyur bcas pa kun/_/slar yang de las 'byung bar byed/_/de las skye bo rnams kyis ni/_/yang dag ma rtogs pa yi phyir/_/tshangs pa'i sgo nga las skyes par/_/
[\[11a.5\]]'khrul pas chos rnams kyis mi bsgul/_/gang gis kyang ni mi shigs pa/_/ji srid 'di ni lus gnas pas/_/las dang las min rab byed pa/_/brtan po 'jigs pa rab spangs pa'i/_/mi shigs thig le bsgom par bshad/_/tshangs pa'i spyod pa bzhi po dang /_/phyi
[\[11a.6\]]rol stong bcas la sogs pa/_/rang gi lha ru bskyed nas kyang /_/phyag rgya bzhis ni rgyas btab pa/_/snga ma bzhin du shes byas nas/_/rim pa 'di yi thig le la/_/rang gi sems ni yang dag bzung /_/rang gi ye shes sems dpa' yi/_/mtshan ma'i dbus gnas sa bon
[\[11a.7\]]las/_/'od zer lnga 'phros de yi rtse/_/dkyil 'khor 'khor lo dpag med sprul/_/de yis khams kun khyab byas nas/_/dbugs kyi rta zhon kun rtog rnams/_/rnam par bsal te de dag kyang /_/dkyil 'khor 'khor lor rab byas te/_/gnyis pa'i dkyil 'khor bsdu
[\[11b\]]
[\[11b.1\]]byas nas/_/ye shes ngo bo sna bug g.yon/_/zhugs byas mtshan ma'i dbus gnas bya/_/sa bon la ni thim pas kyang /_/de ni phyogs dus gnas pa yi/_/sangs rgyas yon tan ci gsungs pa/_/yang dag skyed byed mi shigs pa'i/_/thig le 'od zer lnga 'bar ba/_/rnam par
[\[11b.2\]]gsal byas de las kyang /_/'od zer 'byung bas rang gnas kyang /_/ye shes sems dpa'i nang gsal te/_/de yi phyi yi dkyil 'khor dang /_/nang ni gsal bya de las byung /_/mthe bo'i rtsa dang rje ngar dang /_/brla gnyis dang ni gsang ba'i gnas/_/lte ba dang ni gsus pa
[\[11b.3\]]dang /_/nu ma gnyis dang lag rtse dang /_/mgrin pa dang ni mchu gnyis dang /_/'gram pa gnyis dang mig gnyis dang /_/rna ba'i rtsa dang spyi bo dang /_/tshigs kun thig le AHsogs kyi/_/gzugs su gnas pa bsgrub byas nas/_/mi shigs thig ler thim par bya/_/der ni rang
[\[11b.4\]]gi sems cung zad/_/gzung bas rten dang rten can gyi/_/'khor lor mos byas de dbus su/_/mi shigs thig le ye shes la/_/snang ba'i ngo bo bsgom par bya/_/de yi 'od kyis rang gnas sogs/_/gsal byas ye shes thig le yi/_/nang gsal gzhag pa'i 'od
[\[11b.5\]]zer gyis/_/phyogs bcu 'jig rten khams bzhugs pa'i/_/spyan sngar bdud rtsi zhu byas nas/_/zhal du zhugs nas snying ga yi/_/mi shigs thig ler rab song ste/_/k+ShuM gzugs bdud rtsir rab blangs nas/_/rdo rje'i lam nas phyung nas su/_/'o ma'i rgyun ltar phyogs bcu
[\[11b.6\]]nas/_/'ongs pa yis ni sems can dang /_/sangs rgyas rnams dang mi rgyur bcas/_/yang dag bsdus nas gur sogs zhugs/_/de bzhin chos dbyings phyag rgya dang /_/rten gyi 'khor lor zhugs byas nas/_/de dag yang ni rab bsdus te/_/dkyil 'khor du ni rab
[\[11b.7\]]bsdus nas/_/de yang bdag la bsdu byas te/_/bdag nyid kyang ni mi snang bar/_/ye shes sems dpa'i gnas la dmigs/_/de yang 'khor lo 'khor lo yang /_/ye shes sems dpar zhugs par bya/_/ye shes sems dpa' mi snang nas/_/mtshan ma 'ba' zhig la_
[\[12a\]]
[\[12a.1\]]dmigs bya/_/mtshan ma de yang bsdu byas nas/_/mi shigs thig ler sems bzung ste/_/de las yang ni nang gi tshogs/_/kun bsdus rang snang thig le che/_/'ba' zhig la sems yang dag bzung /_/ci ltar nus bzhin bsgom pas der/_/sems
[\[12a.2\]]ni yang dang yang du zhugs/_/yang ni de las phyir byung ste/_/de yi gnas dang rang gi lus/_/dmigs nas dkyil 'khor 'khor lo dang /_/rten dang khams gsum snang bar bya/_/de nas yang ni gong ma ltar/_/rim par bcug nas thim byas la/_/sems ni thig ler
[\[12a.3\]]gzhag par bya/_/rang gi dbang po der bzung nas/_/sa yi dkyil 'khor chu la zhugs/_/chu de me la de bzhin zhugs/_/me yang rlung la rab tu zhugs/_/rlung yang sems la zhugs par gyur/_/sems ni gnyis med ye shes su/_/cung zad zhugs pas rtags gnas
[\[12a.4\]]pa/_/smig rgyu 'dra dang du ba dang /_/mar me mkha' snang rab 'dra ba/_/sprin med nam mkha' ltar snang ba'i/_/mtshan ma lnga po 'byung bar 'gyur/_/rdo rje sems dpa' zhugs phyir ro/_/thig le la ni sems bzung ste/_/glal zhing dgod dang 'dar la sogs/_/rnal 'byor de
[\[12a.5\]]la gang tshe 'byung /_/thig le yang dag spro byas nas/_/gong ma'i rim pas kun khyab bya/_/'di ni yang dag goms byas pas/_/mi gnas mya ngan 'das pa che/_/thabs kun gyis ni bsgrub bya mchog_/rdo rje 'chang ba chen po thob/_/'di ni lhan cig skyes pa yi/_/ye shes 'ba'
[\[12a.6\]]zhig dbang byas nas/_/rim pa gnyis pa bsgom pa'i thabs/_/mi shigs thig le bsgom pa'o/_/de ltar chos kun de bzhin nyid/_/dpag med dam pa'i phun sum tshogs/_/de dmigs yang dag skyes 'gyur ba/_/bsgom pa'i cho ga rnam bshad nas/_/rnam grangs
[\[12a.7\]]dag kyang yongs su bstan/_/de bzhin nyid dang yang dag mtha'/_/bsam gyis mi khyab pa yi dbyings/_/chos nyid dang ni chos skyon med/_/stong pa nyid dang mtshan ma med/_/smon pa med pa nyid dang yang /_/nyon mongs khur chen 'dor byed pa/_/skye ba med dang 'od gsal
[\[12b\]]
[\[12b.1\]]ba/_/mngon par byang ni chub pa dang /_/gzhan gyi sems shes byed pa dang /_/lha yi rna ba ster ba dang /_/de bzhin lha yi mig ster dang /_/rdzu 'phrul dpag med sprul chen dang /_/dngos po mthar ni phyin pa dang /_/don dam pa yi bden pa dang /_/rdzogs pa yi ni rim pa dang /_/
[\[12b.2\]]yongs su dag pa'i sku gtsang dang /_/kun gyis bstan bya nyid dag dang /_/mkha' ltar rnam par dag pa dang /_/glo bur dri mas mi gos dang /_/gdod nas 'od gsal ba nyid dang /_/gang gis kyang ni mi shigs dang /_/dngos po med pa nyid dang ni/_/rgyu sogs bcu gnyis 'byung
[\[12b.3\]]byed dang /_/dpal chen ye shes yongs dag dang /_/thig le chen po yongs dag dang /_/sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang chen dang /_/nam mkha' nam mkha'i spyod yul dang /_/bsgom pa med pa nyid dang ni/_/rje btsun man ngag chen po dang /_/sna nas rna bar 'pho byed dang /_/nyan thos kyis ni shes min dang /_/
[\[12b.4\]]rang sangs rgyas sogs mi shes dang /_/yi ge med pa nyid dang ni/_/tshig dang bral dang brjod med sogs/_/de la mdo dang rgyud rnams las/_/de 'dra rnam pa mtha' yas pa/_/gsungs shing yang dag gsung 'gyur ba/_/der ni de bzhin nyid 'di las/_/gzhan ni ci yang ma
[\[12b.5\]]gsungs so/_/de bas dad pa sngon 'gro ba'i/_/sems kyis chos kun de bzhin nyid/_/zab gsal gnyis med don chen po/_/rim pa gnyis pa de kho na/_/bla ma'i gsung ni yang dag gzung /_/de bzung gong ma'i rim pa yis/_/rtag tu goms byed skyes bu gang /_/de la brten
[\[12b.6\]]pa'i rtags skyes nas/_/sa nas sar ni 'phar ba ltar/_/de yi rnam pa gong du 'phel/_/rig 'dzin la sogs sprul pa yis/_/gzhan ni don de la sbyor byed/_/de yis brtan 'gyur rnal 'byor pa/_/sgrub pa'i bdag nyid can du 'gyur/_/bdag nyid can des bsgrub pa'i
[\[12b.7\]]mchog_/ji skad gsungs pa brtsam par bya/_/lha mo klu mo gnod sbyin mo/_/mi mo mi'am ci mo'am/_/mkha' 'gro ma la sogs pa rnams/_/rang gi nus pas brtsam par bya/_/smyon pa'i brtul zhugs la sogs pas/_/zla drug sogs par rab tu 'bad/_/de yis rje btsun
[\[13a\]]
[\[13a.1\]]yid med pa/_/dpal ldan sangs rgyas kun ngo bo/_/rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad gnas/_/chos kun de bzhin nyid zab pa/_/sangs rgyas rnams kyi bsgrub bya mchog_/gong ma'i rim pa rnal 'byor pas/_/'bad pa che thang rab byas pas/_/de ltar de ru
[\[13a.2\]]mtshan nyid kyi/_/tshul du cung zad rab gnas pa'i/_/dga' dang dga' ba bar ma dang /_/dga' dang bral ba'i dus su yang /_/ji bzhin gnas pa'i dga' ba gsum/_/ji skad gsungs pa thob par 'gyur/_/de nas mtha' med 'khor ba'i bar/_/rtag pa dang ni mi gdung
[\[13a.3\]]dang /_/bsil ba dang ni gcig pa dang /_/bde ba dang ni dri med dang /_/dga' ba dang ni yid dga' ba/_/'di ni bde chen ro myang brgyad/_/bdag po rdo rje 'chang ba mchog_/rdzogs pa'i rim pa'i rnal 'byor pas/_/bya ba byas pa byed pa byas/_/dbang phyug chen po khur chen
[\[13a.4\]]bor/_/tsher ma dkrugs pa thams cad mkhyen/_/skyes bu dpa' bo cang shes pa/_/glang po chen po dul ba po/_/'khor ba'i mtha' ni pha rol son/_/don dam dang ni kun rdzob kyi/_/bden pa gnyis med rnal 'byor che/_/thab spangs pa'am lam kun rdzogs/_/yon tan
[\[13a.5\]]'byung gnas kun du bzang /_/thams cad 'dus pa'i de kho na/_/sku sogs khams kun 'gengs pa'o/_/gong na med pa yang dag gnas/_/de ltar de sogs rab grags pa/_/ming ni rnam pa mtha' yas pa/_/gnyis med ye shes mtshon pa ste/_/mdo dang rgyud rnams
[\[13a.6\]]thams cad du/_/blo ldan rnams kyis rtogs par bya/_/sa bcu dang ni rab ldan pa'i/_/gong ma'i lha mo rdo rje 'dzin/_/dge ba bcu gsum la gnas pa/_/skad cig gis ni yang dag tu/_/sgrib bral de yis rtogs par byed/_/phreng ba ha ra nu pur sogs/_/mdog dang ku tsa la
[\[13a.7\]]sogs pa/_/pad+ma brtags pa'i dga' shes pa/_/dang por rab tu shes par bya/_/Shadz+dz+rI ni ShA na sogs/_/glu dbyangs bstod dang sid sgra yi/_/snyan pa'i dbyangs kyis dga' 'gyur bas/_/gnyis pa ru ni shes par bya/_/tsan+dan la sogs sna tshogs dris/_/lus byugs lhan cig
[\[13b\]]
[\[13b.1\]]rtsen byed tshe/_/dga' ba yang dag thob byed pa/_/gsum pa ru ni shes par bya/_/ma mchu sbrang rtsis gzhib byas pas/_/mgor gnas byang chub sems 'ju bas/_/ro 'thung dga' bas bdag mnyes pas/_/bzhi par rab tu shes par bya/_/lus la byug cing sna tshogs kyi/_/
[\[13b.2\]]spyod pas rtsen tshe reg bya yis/_/yang dag dga' bar byed pas na/_/lnga pa ru ni shes par bya/_/de yis ye shes rnam pa gsum/_/rig par byed cing rang gi yid/_/yang dag dga' bar rab byed pa/_/drug par shes bya rnal 'byor pas/_/de yi lus ni bdag gi ni/_/rten du gnas
[\[13b.3\]]pa sra ba yis/_/yang dag dga' bar byed pas na/_/bdun pa ru ni shes par bya/_/de yi pad+ma'i zil sogs dang /_/byang sems rlan gyis rang gi sems/_/rab tu dga' bar byed pas na/_/brgyad par rab tu shes par bya/_/gsang gnas drod sogs tsha ba yis/_/bdag
[\[13b.4\]]gi yid ni yang dag par/_/dga' bar byed pa'i mchog yin pas/_/dgu pa ru ni shes par bya/_/de nas bskyod pas ye shes mes/_/phung po khams sogs sreg byed pas/_/yid ni yang dag dga' 'gyur bas/_/bcu par rab tu shes par bya/_/bcu po de yis dang po dang /_/phyis kyi
[\[13b.5\]]'bras bu mchog 'gyur ba/_/gang du gsungs pa rab thob ste/_/de bas de 'dra'i don chen la/_/yang dag 'jug par mi nus pa'i/_/gdul bya rnams la bde gshegs kyis/_/rab tu dga' sogs mtshan nyid du/_/bstan nas de yi don zhugs pas/_/de yis rtogs kyang bla dang bcas/_/
[\[13b.6\]]de nyid dang po'i rnal 'byor la/_/rten dang rten can dkyil 'khor gyi/_/'khor lo rab tu brtan byas nas/_/de zhugs de la brtan byas pas/_/rtogs kyang don 'di ma shes na/_/yang dag sangs rgyas ma yin no/_/'di ni rang byung bcom ldan 'das/_/gcig pu rab tu che ba'i lha/_/
[\[13b.7\]]lhag pa'i lha zhes bya ba ni/_/bcu gsum pa zhes bya bar bshad/_/de ltar rim pa gnyis pa yi/_/de bzhin nyid ni thabs bcas pa'i/_/bdud rtsi mchog 'di rnal 'byor gang /_/'thung bar byed pa sangs rgyas kyi/_/de yi sras su nges pa ste/_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi
[\[14a\]]
[\[14a.1\]]grogs/_/rig pa 'dzin pa'i dpon po ste/_/mkha' 'gro ma yi khyo ru 'gyur/_/nyan thos rang 'dren rnams kyi ni/_/'dren par byed pa'i gtso bo ste/_/sems can phal pa'i rje btsun no/_/de la phyogs bcu khams bzhugs pa'i/_/sangs rgyas byang chub
[\[14a.2\]]sems dpa' dang /_/rig pa'i lha dang khro bo sogs/_/me tog la sogs mchod par bcas/_/zhag gcig skya rengs dang po dang /_/phyed ni dros pa'i dus nyid dang /_/chal chil mtshams su nam mkha' las/_/mchod pa byas nas sngags brjod cing /_/rang gi zhing du
[\[14a.3\]]'gro bar 'gyur/_/de bas dag pa'i lha rnams kyang /_/de bzhin du ni mchod byed na/_/ma dag pa yi lha rnams ni/_/de la ci yi phyir mi mchod/_/sems can phal pa gzhan gyis ni/_/me tog snyim pa bkang nas ni/_/mgrin pa dma' bas zhabs 'dud cing /_/rtag tu bkur
[\[14a.4\]]bar shin tu 'os/_/de ni skyes bu rkang gnyis gtso/_/kun mkhyen rnams kyis bzhag pa ste/_/phyin log khur chen por byed pas/_/ma 'ongs rdo rje 'chang ba ste/_/de la brnyas byed sems can gang /_/sgrub pa po de glang dang 'dra/_/de yis nga la brnyas byed pas/_/ngas ni
[\[14a.5\]]de kun dus kun spong /_/cig shos lus la ngag nas phyir/_/mchod cing brjod pas lus rnams kyi/_/sgrib pa de yis dag byed do/_/rim pa gnyis 'dir sgrub pa po/_/rtse gcig pa yis rnam par gzung /_/de gzung tshe 'di nyid la yang /_/brtul zhugs cho ga nyid kyis ni/_/
[\[14a.6\]]lha mos rkyen ni rab byas te/_/phyag rgya chen po rang rgyud la/_/'pho bar the tshom mi bya'o/_/da ni rang nyid byin brlabs pa'i/_/rim pa 'di ni rnal 'byor pa/_/bya bas bskal pa 'ga' zhig la/_/yang dag tu ni bshad par bya/_/gang zhig bla ma mnyes byas nas/_/des gnang
[\[14a.7\]]dam sdom bcas pa ru/_/bum pa la sogs rab thob ste/_/bla ma'i zhal las rnyed pa yi/_/de bzhin nyid ni rab thob cing /_/gsang dang mchog tu gsang rigs pas/_/ji skad bshad pa'i bya ba yis/_/yang dag bsgom ni mi nus pas/_/ji bzhin pa yi de kho na/_/rim pa 'di
[\[14b\]]
[\[14b.1\]]yis bsgom par bya/_/gang zhig dus ni phyi zhig la/_/'chi ba'i mtshan ma bdag gis mthong /_/'chi bar gyur pa'i dus byung na/_/nad kyis yang dag ma rnyogs par/_/'pho ba'i sbyor ba yang dag bya/_/dpral ba dang ni lte ba dang /_/spyi gtsug dang ni mig dang ni/_/rna ba dang ni
[\[14b.2\]]sna dag dang /_/chu yi gnas dang chu min gnas/_/kha yi gnas dang ye shes kyi/_/'gro 'ong gis ni rtags shes bya/_/dpral ba gzugs kyi khams kyi ni/_/rtags skyes pa ru shes par bya/_/lte bar 'dod khams lha rnams kyi/_/rtags byung de ru skye bar nges/_/spyi
[\[14b.3\]]gtsug gzugs med khams rnams kyi/_/rtags byung de ru skye bar 'gyur/_/rna gnyis ye shes 'pho ba na/_/gnod sbyin gnas su skye bar 'gyur/_/sna gnyis rig pa 'dzin pa yi/_/gnas su nges par 'gro ba'o/_/mig gnyis mi rnams rgyal por 'gyur/_/rtags
[\[14b.4\]]ni yang dag skye bar 'gyur/_/kha ru ye shes 'pho ba na/_/yi dgas rtags su shes par bya/_/chu gnas dud 'gro rnams kyi ni/_/rtags su yang dag rab shes bya/_/chu min bu gar ye shes 'gro/_/dmyal ba'i rtags su shes par bya/_/de ltar ye shes 'pho ba yi/_/rnam
[\[14b.5\]]pa'i cha ni shes byas nas/_/sgrogs pa lnga yi yi ge yis/_/steng gi sgo bdun dgag par bya/_/chu yi sgo ru suM gis dgag_/chu min k+ShuM gis dgag par bya/_/de ltar sgo dgu bkag nas kyang /_/rim pa 'di yis rang sems kyi/_/gnas ni rab tu btsal byas pas/_/dbyings
[\[14b.6\]]nyid du ni nges par 'gro/_/phung po skye mched khams rnams su/_/rnal 'byor rgyud kyis dpyad pa ltar/_/rnam par bsgom byas ye shes so/_/gong na med pa rtogs par 'gyur/_/bdag nyid ji skad gsungs pa bzhin/_/lha yi lus su gyur byas pa/_/chos kyi dbyings dang rnam
[\[14b.7\]]shes dang /_/bdag nyid sangs rgyas skur byas pa'i/_/gnas ni rin chen sna tshogs pa'i/_/kha dog sna lngas rab brgyan pa'i/_/rdo rje rtse mo dgu pa mchog_/bdag gi spyi bo'i steng du ni/_/bsams nas de ru rang gi sems/_/rdo rje dkar po bcu tshal tsam/_/rtse lnga bsams
[\[15a\]]
[\[15a.1\]]nas brtag par bya/_/yar gyi rtse lnga thabs lnga ste/_/de bzhin mar bltas shes rab lnga/_/dbus kyi bum pa ri bong can/_/bsams nas de ru ye shes che/_/ser po byang chub sems 'dra ba/_/'dzag pa'i ngang tshul dang 'dra ba/_/thig le tsa na ka yi 'bru/_/lnga
[\[15a.2\]]'byor tshad du bsgom par bya/_/de nas chos kun thams cad kun/_/med par bsams nas bdag dmigs te/_/bdag kyang bdag la thim byas nas/_/sems tsam de yang mda' bzhin du/_/spyi bor rdo rje 'og cha yi/_/sbu gur zhugs nas thig ler thim/_/de ni de bzhin
[\[15a.3\]]gshegs pa rnams/_/lha mo rnams kyi rang bzhin gyi/_/gnas su shes par rab tu bya/_/de ni gdod nas grub pa'i gzugs/_/de ru shes pa rab zhugs pa/_/sems de yang dang yang du gzung /_/de las sems de yar ba ltar/_/rdo rje rtse dgu steng cha yi/_/sbu gur byung nas
[\[15a.4\]]sna tshogs kyi/_/pad+mar zla ba gnas pa la/_/rdo rje sems dpa'i skur gyur te/_/mtshan dang dpe byad kun brgyan pa/_/rgyan kun brgyan pa'i na bza' dang /_/bral nas shin tu gsal dmigs te/_/de gnyis med pa'i sbyor ba yis/_/byin rlabs las byung 'khor lo che/_/rnam par
[\[15a.5\]]'phro zhing 'du bar bsam/_/de ltar rnam par bsgom pa mchog_/yang dang yang du ci nus bsgom/_/bsam pa de yi rkyen gyis ni/_/bdag sems dbyings su zhugs pa'i tshe/_/gsal zhing rab dag mkha' 'dra rtogs/_/de nas rdzu 'phrul shugs ldan pa/_/lo lnga lon pa'i byis pa'i
[\[15a.6\]]gzugs/_/'grub tshe dpe med bde rdzogs rtogs/_/de las skye gnas gzhan du ni/_/'phel bar byed tshe sprul pa'i gzugs/_/yang dag tu ni rtogs par 'gyur/_/de lta bas na sems can gyi/_/bsam pa gang dang gang dag gis/_/mi rnams yid ni yang dag sbyor/_/de dang de ni
[\[15a.7\]]mdo bzhin du/_/sna tshogs nor bu lta bur 'gyur/_/chos sku rab dga' mkha' mnyam pa/_/shi dang brgyal dang gnyid log dang /_/glal dang 'khrig dus skad cig tsam/_/myong bar 'gyur bas rab bsgoms na/_/lus can rnams ni yid ni sbyong /_/cho ga 'di yis sems can gang /_/
[\[15b\]]
[\[15b.1\]]mtshams med byed cing rmongs pa yi/_/skye bo bram ze gsod pa yang /_/de yis mi 'grub cung zad med/_/de bas bka' lung rab thob nas/_/dam sdom rnam par bsrung byas te/_/sku gsum 'grub par the tshom med/_/gal te sku gsum ma grub na/_/rig pa 'dzin pa'i
[\[15b.2\]]gtsor 'gyur te/_/rim gyis phyag rgya chen por 'gyur/_/de ltar rnam pa gsum gyis ni/_/dngos grub de ni bsgom pa bshad/_/gang zhig 'di ni ma rtogs par/_/gsang ba smra bar byed pa ni/_/de ni nga dang de bzhin gshegs/_/nam zhig de la sbyar byas pas/_/byin gyis
[\[15b.3\]]rlob par mi byed do/_/'di ni don ldan 'ga' zhig la/_/nga ni de yi lus gnas te/_/bsgrub pa gzhan la mchod pa len/_/de yis de mnyes rang gi rgyud/_/las kyi sgrib pa dag byed do/_/'di don rna bar 'pho byed pa/_/gang gi dus su gnas pa der/_/sangs rgyas bstan
[\[15b.4\]]pa rin chen yang /_/gnas pa rab tu bshad pa yin/_/brgyud pa'i rim pa 'di chad nas/_/sangs rgyas bstan pa nub pa ru/_/kun gyis rab tu shes par bya/_/de bas khyod kyi yid gcig tu/_/yang dag bsdus la ma 'ongs pa'i/_/gang zag sngon du tshogs bskyed pa'i/_/

[\[23a.1\]]mda'/_/sems can thams cad tshim par byed pas na/_/ut+pal sngon po nyes kun gnyen po dang /_/yon tan thams cad 'dzin par byed pa'i gzhu/_/rnam pa sna tshogs mchog rnams kyis brgyan cing /_/yid du 'ong ba'i rin chen mchog gis brgyan/_/sangs rgyas

[\[23b.1\]]drug rdzogs pa'i rnal 'byor par/_/gyur te nye ba yi ni sgrub pa rdzogs/_/reg pa'o/_/rdo rje gsum rdzogs nges par gnas don du/_/zla gsum snying ga lkog ma mgo bor yang /_/brang dang lkog ma'i bar du bzhi pa dgod/_/sna tshogs pad+ma rgyas pa'i dbus gnas pa'i/_/hUM gi rdo rje las

[\[24a\]]
[\[24a.1\]]sgrub yan lag_/sngags spangs brjod de sems kyis dbang bskur te/_/dpal ldan ye shes sems dpa' rtag tu bskul/_/gang phyir 'di ni rdo rje 'dzin rgyud gsungs/_/shes rab rno can de rnams kyis rab sgrub/_/tshor ba'o/_/bdag gis bdag snying ye shes 'od tshogs
[\[24a.2\]]kyis/_/mkha' bzhugs rgyal ba ma lus yang dag bskul/_/de yi lus nang byung ba'i 'od zer las/_/gzugs sogs rdo rje rang byung gzhan yang ni/_/dpal ldan mA ma kI dang gos dkar can/_/sgrol ma zhes bya lha mo de rnams ni/_/rnga yi sgra ldan rnams kyi sgra sgrogs shing /_/byug pa la sogs
[\[24a.3\]]me tog phreng thogs shing /_/gser gyi bum pa ye shes chus gang ba/_/bkra shis bum pa lag thogs klu rnams kyis/_/rang gtso cod pan thogs shing mkha' dkyil gnas/_/mchog tu dbang bskur bar ni dbab par bya/_/bab 'gyur de nyid las ni byung ba yi/_/mi bskyod rdo rje cod pan dag tu
[\[24a.4\]]gnas/_/mthong na shin tu sems ni rnam dag par/_/gyur pa de nyid sgrub pa chen po'o/_/srid pa'o/_/rig ma mtshan mchog yon tan kun ldan pa/_/rang gi sa bon las byung kun du rtog_/dkyil 'khor mngon sum du ni rab tu gzhag_/de la bsnyen pa la sogs des byas bdag_/sa snying la

[\[27a.1\]]ral gri/_/maM las byung ba'i sems kyi me bsgoms te/_/rdo rje gsum sku dang yang mnyam por byung /_/de rnams snying gnas rang mtshan sa bon las/_/byung nas ye shes 'od zer rab gsal ba'i/_/'od kyis ma lus sna tshogs kun du gang /_/ye shes bdud rtsi rgyun gyi rjes

[\[27b.1\]]de nyid sa bon las 'dir sangs rgyas spro/_/'od zer tshogs de nam mkhar song nas kyang /_/de nas byung ba'i lha mo de rnams kyis/_/dam tshig ces bya'i 'khor la mchod par byed/_/thams cad kun du 'khyud par gyur pa dang /_/dga' ba dag gis sangs rgyas rnams 'khyud 'gyur/_/de nas rang

[\[27b.7\]]tshim par bya/_/nang gi bdag nyid kyis ni sbyin sreg las/_/mthar thug par yang sems kyi bya ba ste/_/phung po la sogs bud shing kun dang ldan/_/ye shes me 'bar ba yis phung po ni/_/bsregs pa gang yin de ni bla med bshad/_/ma lus 'dod pa yi ni cho ga nyid/_/de yis rang gi lha yi rnam_
[\[28a\]]
[\[28a.1\]]par bsgom par bya/_/rang dang gzhan lus la yang kun du mchod/_/sangs rgyas rnams bsten dam tshig shin tu thob/_/rjes su mthun pa'i 'gro ba'i don byas shing /_/de bzhin gshegs rnams kun du mchod par bsam/_/sems ni gcig tu mnyam par gzhag gyur pas/_/

[\[28a.3\]]'byung 'gyur bud med mthong ba las/_/khyi dang 'dod pa can dang rab byung gsum/_/bde dang sdug bsngal rnam par grol ba'i sems/_/lus la sogs pa'i dge dang mi dge'i las/_/gang phyir de ni sems kyi dbang gis gsungs/_/de bas rtag tu rnam rtog dra gcod pa'i/_/sems ni nag po'i las

[\[28a.5\]]dbang bskur bas ni nyes kun dang /_/'gro ba rang bzhin gyis ni dag par blta/_/phyi rol khrus la'ang cho ga 'dis bya'o/_/gang zhig thun mtshams nyams par gyur pa yis/_/des kyang cho ga 'di ni bya ba ste/_/ji lta ba bzhin nyes pa gsum 'byung gsungs/_/gang yang sna tshogs pad+ma'i dbus
[\[28a.6\]]gnas pa'i/_/hUM las byung ba yi ni bgegs mthar byed/_/bdud rtsi zhes bya 'khor lo dbang bskur bas/_/'bad pas bgegs rnams thams cad gzhom bya ste/_/de ltar ting 'dzin gsum po bsgom bdag nyid/_/gang bsgoms pas ni shin tu skyo gyur nas/_/'khor lo rang snying nang zhugs rnam
[\[28a.7\]]par bsam/_/rnal 'byor ldan pas rig mar ldan par nyal/_/rnal 'byor gnyid log ldang ba'i dus su ni/_/lha mo'i tshogs kyis blangs pa'i glu yi sgras/_/myur bar kun du langs nas yang byas te/_/sngar bshad pa yi mnyam par gzhag par bya/_/dngos grub mtshan ma nye bar brtags nas ni/_/
[\[28b\]]
[\[28b.1\]]khang bzangs ngos gnyis nas ni 'dzeg pa dang /_/dag pa'i gtsug lag khang dang sangs rgyas sku/_/rmi lam gzhon nu ma dang rgyal po mthong /_/de nyid gsum gyi cho ga bzhin mchod nas/_/dngos grub 'dod pa yis ni dkyil 'khor bya/_/rig pa 'dzin dang ri lu mig sman dang /_/bcud kyis len
[\[28b.2\]]pa'am phyag rgya che la sogs/_/rta dang gser dang rin chen sa gzhi 'gro/_/khrag dang bu dang bu mo du ma byin/_/bskal pa grangs med gsum la sogs pa yis/_/'di ru la las sangs rgyas thob par 'gyur/_/gang yang bde ba chen po'i ting nge 'dzin/_/thams cad bsgoms pas bde bar
[\[28b.3\]]nyer bsgoms nas/_/de steng sdig pa kun las rnam grol nas/_/skad cig gis te rdo rje 'dzin par 'gyur/_/bdag gis man ngag brtsams 'di rab dad pas/_/bla ma'i zhal gyi pad+ma las rnyed de/_/mkhas pa rnams kyis 'di la ltad mo gyis/_/'gro ba kun la phan phyir bdag gis byas/_/ji ltar
[\[28b.4\]]log pa'i brdzun gyis byas pa yis/_/pha yi drung nas cung zad rnyed pa ltar/_/de bzhin bdag gis bsod nams cung zad rnyed/_/de nas 'jig rten 'jam pa'i rdo rjer shog_/dpal ldan u rgyan yul du brten skyes shing /_/dpag med rgyud don ma lus rab mkhyen pa/_/dpal ldan rnam par dul zhi'i
[\[28b.5\]]zhal snga nas/_/de yis dbang bskur slob ma'i gtso bo mchog_/de las sin d+hU'i ngos su de skyes shing /_/rnam thos bsti gnas zhes bshad rgyal bzhugs nas/_/shAkya'i bshes gnyen bdag nyid sangs rgyas shing /_/de yis yongs bkrol zhal gyi man ngag go/_/dpal ldan u rgyan
[\[28b.6\]]yul nas byung ba'i sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyi zhal snga nas kyi sgrub thabs kyi man ngag rdzogs so//_//lo tsA ba dge slong khyung wer rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//[{D1855}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_sa man+ta b+ha dra nA ma sA d+ha naM/_
[\[28b.7\]]bod skad du/_kun du bzang po zhes bya ba'i sgrub pa'i thabs/_bcom ldan 'das 'jam pa'i rdo rje la phyag 'tshal lo/_/dpal ldan mi shes kun spangs dri med gzi brjid ldan/_/dpag med rigs kyi sprul pa rnams kyis rab brgyan cing /_/shes rab yan lag 'dus pas 'bar zhing rnam mdzes
[\[29a\]]
[\[29a.1\]]pa/_/'jam dpal gang de mchod phyir de la phyag 'tshal lo/_/dpal ldan 'dus pa'i gzhung lugs bshes gnyen ni/_/dam pa yis ni bskul phyir spro byas te/_/'gro ba ma lus don ni phun tshogs pa'i/_/rgyur gyur cho ga bdag gis bshad par bya/_/dal 'byor 'di ni shin tu

[\[29a.3\]]tshul dag la ni lhag par mos/_/dpal ldan 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor cho ga yis/_/rang gi dbang bskur phun sum tshogs ldan zhing /_/cho ga bzhin du rjes gnang thob pa yi/_/blo dang ldan pas rang sngags mnyes par bya/_/la la dri med chu ni phun tshogs shing /_/shing mchog mdzes pas rnam par brgyan pa yi/_/

[\[29a.6\]]sdig pa dag ni bshags pa la sogs bya/_/gang zhig thog med srid pa'i chu klung du/_/ma lus kun rtog gis bsags rnyog pa rnams/_/thugs rje che ldan spyan sngar de dag ni/_/cho ga bzhin du thams cad bshags par bgyi/_/rdzogs sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dang /_/'phags pa gzhan

[\[29b.4\]]mnyam med pa/_/sngags pas cho gas de ltar bsgom par bya/_/ngo bo nyid dang bral phyir stong pa ste/_/rang bzhin rgyu dang bral bas mtshan ma med/_/rtog pa rnams dang bral phyir dngos po ni/_/ma lus smon pa las ni nges par grol/_/oM shU n+ya tA dz+nyA na badzra swa b+hA ba At+ma ko\u0f85haM/_de 'og hUM gis

[\[30a.1\]]pa yi/_/rlung gis bskyod pa'i ba dan phreng ba dang /_/dril bu sgra sgrogs phyogs sgo kun khyab pa/_/gang phyir dam chos gsung rab yan lag dgu/_/gdul bya thams cad la ni skyob pa po/_/me long dra ba dra phyed me tog gi_/phreng ba sna tshogs kyis brgyan mnyam pa med/_/ye

[\[30a.6\]]'drar dkar ba'i mdangs ldan zhing /_/g.yas dang g.yon pa'i zhal ni sngo dang dmar/_/sna tshogs rgyan rnams 'bar ba'i phyag gnyis kyis/_/rig ma dam par 'khyud par mdzad pa'o/_/lhag ma'i phyag gis rdo rje ral gri dang /_/pad+ma rin chen bsnams pas zung gnyis mdzes/_/khams gsum

[\[30b.1\]]dpag med kyis/_/'dul ba'i 'jig rten thams cad dmigs nas ni/_/dga' ba'i sgyu ma'i sgra yis de rnams dang /_/rgyal ba'i tshogs rnams ma lus gzhug par bya/_/de ni spyan la sogs pa'i lha mo dang /_/gzugs sogs ma lus yul gyi rang bzhin du/_/phyung nas rig ma de dag thams cad ni/_/

[\[30b.4\]]reg bya dang ni chos dbyings rdo rje dang /_/sa dang chu dang me dang rlung rnams ni/_/ngo bo nyid gyur spyan la sogs par grags/_/gzugs dang tshor ba de bzhin 'du shes dang /_/'du byed dang ni rnam par shes bshad pa/_/rnam par snang mdzad la sogs bde gshegs te/_/de rjes sa bon gyis ni dbyung bar bya/_/k+ShiM
[\[30b.5\]]dzrIM khaM gaM Sh+kaM saM zhes bshad pa/_/'di dag mig la sogs pa rnams kyi ming /_/dzaHhUM baM hoH khaM raM zhes bshad pa/_/de dag gzugs kyi rdo rje la sogs pa/_/laM mAM paM tAM zhes bya bzhir bshad pa/_/de dag spyan la sogs pa rnams kyi yin/_/b+h+rUM AM dzrAM khaM hUM zhes bya ba 'di/_/rim pa ji bzhin rtag pa la sogs
[\[30b.6\]]pa'i 'o/_/oM AH hUM zhes bya ba'i sems nyid ni/_/'od ldan hoH dang spel ba cho ga bzhin/_/pad+ma'i nang du zhugs pa mnyam med pa/_/shes rab chags pas zhu bar byas par bsam/_/de yi 'od kyi mthu yis gnyis ka yang /_/zla ba zhu bar byas par mthong ba dang /_/spyan la sogs pa'i lha mo
[\[30b.7\]]rnams kyis ni/_/glu yi sgra yis bskul bar byas par bsam/_/sems can khams na gnas kyi dbang phyug khyod ni rdo rje'i thugs/_/dga' ba yid 'ong don chen 'dod pas bdag la bskyab tu gsol/_/mgon po gal te de ring bdag ni gson par mchis bzhed na/_/sems can yab chen

[\[31a.1\]]gnyen mchog bdag la dgyes par mdzad du gsol/_/rdo rje'i sku khyod bka' yi 'khor lo sems can kun la phan/_/sangs rgyas don du byang chub don dam rab tu phan par gzigs/_/mgon po gal te de ring bdag ni gson par mchis bzhed na/_/'dod chags dam tshig chags
[\[31a.2\]]pas bdag la dgyes par mdzad du gsol/_/khyod ni rdo rje'i gsung ste kun la phan zhing thugs brtse ba/_/'jig rten dag gi don dang dgos pa mdzad la rab tu brtson/_/mgon po gal te de ring bdag ni gson par mchis bzhed na/_/dga' ba'i spyod pa kun du bzang po bdag la dgyes par mdzad du gsol/_/

[\[31a.7\]]wa At+ma ko\u0f85haM/_de 'og sa snying sa bon 'od rnams kyis/_/rang gi mig sogs sa snying la sogs pas/_/ji bzhin bkang nas dri med rang zla yis/_/rdo rje lte ba'i dbus gnas yi ge hUM/_/thugs kyi rdo rje'i de bzhin kha dang ni/_/mgo por pad+ma 'khor lo la gnas pa'i/_/AH dang oM ni gsung gi
[\[31b\]]
[\[31b.1\]]rdo rje dang /_/sku yi rdo rje nyid du bsam par bya/_/de yi thugs ka'i 'od kyi tshogs rnams dang /_/shes rab dam par gnas pa'i 'od rnams kyis/_/kun nas rgyal ba'i dbang po mchod nas ni/_/thugs kyi rdo rje la sogs byin gyis brlab/_/dpal ldan rdo rje thugs 'chang ba/_/rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms

[\[31b.3\]]ko\u0f85haM/_/chos kyi gsung lam dpal dang ldan/_/rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms pas/_/deng bdag byin gyis brlabs nas su/_/rdo rje gsung gis mdzad du gsol/_/phyogs bcur bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams/_/rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms pas/_/deng bdag byin gyis brlabs nas su/_/
