[\[31b.7\]]nyid ni yang dag blta/_/mig la sogs pa dgang zhing yi ge gsum/_/rnam par bkod pas lus ni 'od dang ldan/_/de nyid shes pas mgo dang snying ga dang /_/lte ba gsang ba de bzhin brla gnyis sogs/_/oM hUM swA AH hA zhes grags pa rnams/_/de ni sku thugs rdo rje bzang rigs sogs/_/lnga po
[\[32a\]]
[\[32a.1\]]rnams kyis yan lag byin brlabs te/_/'od kyi phreng ba dam pas 'gro gsum khyab/_/AH yis sna tshogs pad+ma'i lte ba bya/_/hUM gis 'dab ma brgyad pa rnam par sprul/_/shes rab dam pa'i rgyu mthun ngo bo nyid/_/thabs dang bcas par 'byung ba'i rang gi lus/_/de yis
[\[32a.2\]]bde gshegs rjes su mnyes bya zhes/_/sngags pas dga' ba kun du brtsam par bya/_/oM sarba ta thA ga tA nu rA ga na badzra swa b+hA wa At+ma ko\u0f85haM/_thugs ka'i zla ba'i sngags kyi 'od rnams kyis/_/ma lus sangs rgyas tshogs rnams bcug nas ni/_/hUM gi rdo rje las byung dri ma med pa yi/_/yid tshul
[\[32a.3\]]dam pa'i chu skyes la gnas pa/_/rang gi snying po las byung ma lus pa'i/_/rang gi dkyil 'khor pa yi gzugs bsams la/_/cho ga 'di yis sems ni brtan po dang /_/'jig rten rnams la phan phyir yang dag dbyung /_/badzra d+h+r-ika ces bya dang thugs rdo rje/_/skye bo dam pa'i don mdzad yang dag
[\[32a.4\]]bskul/_/nor bu sngon po'i 'od 'drar yang dag 'bar/_/g.yas dang g.yon pa'i zhal ni dkar dang dmar/_/dam pa dang po lta bu'i phyag dang ldan/_/kha dog dpag tu med pa'i 'od tshogs mnga'/_/blo dang ldan pas legs bsdus bdag nyid kyi/_/dngos po thams cad kyis ni zhugs par bya/_/dzi na dzika
[\[32a.5\]]ces bya ba sku rdo rje/_/rdo rje 'dzin 'dra'i sku mdog zhal gyis mdzes/_/'khor lo la sogs phyag mtshan rnams de bzhin/_/shar gyi pad+mar zla ba'i dbus su bsam/_/rat+na d+h+r-ika ces bya ba 'di yis ni/_/lho ru rin chen 'byung zhal gzhon nu 'dra/_/btso ma'i gser gyi mdangs dang 'dra ba la/_/phyag drug
[\[32a.6\]]margad rin chen la sogs bsnams/_/A ro l-i ka 'od dpag med pad+ma ni/_/rA ga ltar dmar zhal gnyis de dang 'dra/_/'od zer 'bar zhing phyag na pad+ma sogs/_/mtshan ma bsnams pa nub tu bsam par bya/_/pradz+nyA d+h+r-ika ces bya bas don yod grub/_/rin chen ma rgad lta bu'i mdog ldan zhing /_/
[\[32a.7\]]snga ma lta bu'i zhal sogs phun tshogs mnga'/_/ral gri la sogs bsnams pa byang du bsam/_/ral pa cod pan mdzes dang sna tshogs pa'i/_/rin chen mchog gi 'od zer 'bar bas brgyan/_/rig ma'i mgon dang rab tu bcas pa'i sku/_/thams cad nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor dag la bsam/_/mo
[\[32b\]]
[\[32b.1\]]ha ra tI zhes pas lha mo spyan/_/zla ba'i dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa la gnas pa/_/mchog tu sgeg cing sku yi rdo rje 'dra/_/me yi phyogs nyid du ni bsam par bya/_/dwe Sha ra tI zhes pa dga' ba che/_/dga' chen mchog 'dod mA ma kI zhes pa/_/zhal mdzes phyag rnams thugs kyi gtso 'dra ba/_/rnam par
[\[32b.2\]]sgeg pa bden bral mtshams su bsam/_/rA ga ra tI zhes bya'i yum mchog ni/_/gos dkar yon tan rin chen mtha' yas pa/_/dri med sku ni gsung gi dbang phyug 'dra/_/rlung gi phyogs su rnam par bsam par bya/_/badzra ra tIs rab bskul sgrol ma ni/_/dri med rin chen 'od kyi phreng ba yis/_/phyogs
[\[32b.3\]]kyi chogs khebs rang gi ngo bo ni/_/rin chen dbang 'dra dbang ldan phyogs su bsam/_/lha mo 'di rnams nges pa'i phyag mtshan ni/_/'khor lo bzang dang ut+pal dmar po dang /_/pad+ma ut+pal gser mdog rim bzhin bsam/_/lhag ma rnams ni bdag po ji bzhin 'dod/_/de nyid gsum gyis
[\[32b.4\]]gzugs kyi rdo rje sogs/_/lha mo rnams ni sku la sogs 'dra bar/_/dkyil 'khor gyi ni mtshams gyur bzhi po dang /_/rtsa ba'i sgo yi ngos gnyis dag tu bsam/_/ya mAn+ta kr-ita ces byas gshin rje gshed/_/mtha' yas 'jigs 'od phyogs kun khyab dang ldan/_/dus mtha' mi bzad sprin
[\[32b.5\]]gyi dkyil 'khor mdog_/thugs kyi rgyal po dag dang sku mtshungs pa/_/drag po'i rigs 'od dpag med rnam 'phro bas/_/gshin rje mthar mdzad shin tu gdug pa yi/_/sbrul gyis lus kyi yan lag rnam brgyan pa/_/dpal ldan shar gyi sgor ni bsam par bya/_/pradz+nyAn+ta kr-ita ces byas bla med
[\[32b.6\]]'od/_/drag cing phyag sogs sku yi rdo rje 'dra/_/gzhan gyis mi thub ces bya gtum po ni/_/lho phyogs kyi ni sgo ru bsam par bya/_/pad+mAn+ta kr-ita ces byas phyogs rnams kyi/_/'khor lo'i 'od kyis mngon par khebs byed pa/_/'od mdangs 'jig dus me 'drar 'jigs par ldan/_/phyag la
[\[32b.7\]]sogs par gsung gi rdo rje 'dra/_/gdug pa du ma rnam gnon 'jigs pa'i zhal/_/thub dbang ha ha zhes ni bzhad pa yis/_/ri bor bcas pa sgyel bas skrag mdzad pa/_/rta mgrin de bzhin nub kyi phyogs su bsam/_/big+hAt+ta kr-ita ces byas dpa' bo ni/_/dus mtha'i me ltar drag po bdud rtsi
[\[33a\]]
[\[33a.1\]]'khyil/_/'phags pa'i zhal sogs mi bskyod dang mtshungs pa/_/de bzhin byang gi sgo ru bsam par bya/_/rnam par snang mdzad thugs gtso 'od dpag med/_/thugs kyi dbang po rim bzhin cod pan yin/_/tho ba dbyug pa de bzhin pad+ma dang /_/rdo rje sogs 'di phyag ni
[\[33a.2\]]kun la bsam/_/de ltar yongs su rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor la/_/dngos po thams cad kyis ni bltas nas kyang /_/snying po'i sngags kyi 'od zer lcags kyu yis/_/drangs nas bde bar gshegs rnams bsgom par bya/_/shes rab thabs kyi rang bzhin dri med pa'i/_/ting 'dzin las byung dam pa'i
[\[33a.3\]]bdes gang bar/_/'khor lo bsams nas de nas gshin rje ni/_/mthar byed la sogs bshad pas bsrung bar bya/_/rang gi snying pos mngon bzlas mchod yon ni/_/tsan+dan bzang sogs me tog gis mdzes dbul/_/rang las byas pa lta bur dbang bskur zhing /_cho ga yis ni mngon par mchod
[\[33a.4\]]par bya/_/bad nang rang gi sa bon 'di rnams kyis/_/gzugs la sogs pa thams cad drangs nas ni/_/yang dag byang chub yid kyi ngo bo yis/_/'od kyi dkyil 'khor dag tu bsgom par bya/_/shes rab ba spu re re las byung ba'i/_/'od zer rnam pa sna tshogs rgya chen tshogs/_/ma lus nam mkha'i
[\[33a.5\]]gtos ni kun du khyab/_/de la blo dang ldan pas rab tu spro/_/'od kyi sgo las nges par byung ba yi/_/yan lag dri med rgyan kun gyis legs brgyan/_/me long pi wang dri dang ro yi snod/_/gos dang chos 'byung ba la sogs pa yi/_/mtshan mas rim gyis rnam par sgeg bcas shing /_/rol pa'i
[\[33a.6\]]lag pa dam pa rnams dang ni/_/'od kyi snang bas sprul pa sna tshogs pa'i/_/mchod pa'i sprin gyi dra bas khyab pa dang /_/dngos rnams sgyu ma la sogs so sor ni/_/yang dag rig cing 'jig rten blta mkhas pa/_/rtog pa ma lus kun las nges grol zhing /_/mchog tu bde ba bskyed pa'i rgyur gyur
[\[33a.7\]]pa/_/gzugs la sogs pa'i lha mo rnams dang ni/_/de bzhin phyi yi dri sogs thams cad kyis/_/rgyal ba'i dbang po rnams ni legs mchod cing /_/de ltar tha dad rtogs las nges grol bya/_/oM sarba ta thA ga ta pU dza badzra swa b+hA wa At+ma ko\u0f85haM/_sgra yi yul rnams ma lus pa rnams ni/_/brag
[\[33b\]]
[\[33b.1\]]ca'i sgra 'drar nges brtags de rjes la/_/rang yid lhag pa'i lha ru gnas pa la/_/chos rnams bstod pa'i sgra ni byed par bsam/_/mi bskyod rdo rje ye shes che/_/rdo rje dbyings ni mkha' chen po/_/rdo rje gsum mchog dkyil 'khor gsum/_/rdo rje dbyangs la phyag 'tshal lo/_/rnam par snang
[\[33b.2\]]mdzad dag pa che/_/rdo rje zhi ba dga' chen po/_/rang bzhin 'od gsal mchog gi mchog_/ston pa rdo rjer phyag 'tshal lo/_/rin chen rgyal po rab tu zab/_/rdo rje nam mkha' dri med mkha'/_/rang bzhin dag pa gos pa med/_/rdo rje'i sku la phyag 'tshal lo/_/rdo rje mi 'chi rgyal po che/_/mi rtog nam
[\[33b.3\]]mkha' rdo rje 'dzin/_/'dod chags pha rol phyin pa brnyes/_/rdo rje'i gsung la phyag 'tshal lo/_/don yod rdo rje rdzogs sangs rgyas/_/bsam pa thams cad rdzogs mdzad pa/_/rang bzhin dag pa nyid las byung /_/rdo rje sems dpa' phyag 'tshal lo/_/'bar ba'i oM gyi byin rlabs rlung dang me'i/_/
[\[33b.4\]]dkyil 'khor la gnas rab sbar bdud rtsi lnga/_/de nas yi ge gsum bzlas dpag med pa'i/_/thub pa'i dbang po'i nang du chud par bya/_/ye shes bdud rtsi'i ngo bor bsams nas ni/_/hUM dgod rdo rje'i lce ni bzang po dang /_/snying ga'i zla ba'i dbus su ma lus pa'i/_/rgyal ba'i 'khor lo des ni tshim
[\[33b.5\]]par bya/_/snying po'i 'od zer dpag med kyis sprul pa'i/_/thub pas mi shes kun du nges bsal nas/_/'gro ba ma lus rdzogs sangs rgyas byas te/_/rang gi gsang sngags nang du chud par bya/_/gzugs la sogs pa'i rnam pa dang bral bas/_/'dzin pa de ni mngon sum mthong mi nus/_/gzung ba
[\[33b.6\]]rnams kyang cung zad yod min la/_/gzhan pa'i 'brel pa yis kyang mthong ba med/_/bde sogs de ni yongs su 'dzin pa ni/_/bya ba 'ga' yang yod par ma mthong ste/_/cig car shes pa'i phyir na gzugs sogs bzhin/_/'di dag 'dzin pa por ni yod ma yin/_/dkar po la sogs gang zhig
[\[33b.7\]]mthong ba rnams/_/de nyid dus gzhan dag tu mthong mi 'gyur/_/'di nyid rtag tu gcig la gcig 'gal ba/_/yin phyir bde ba la sogs dag dang mtshungs/_/thog mtha' la sogs bye brag snang bas na/_/gzugs la sogs pa 'di dag gcig ma yin/_/phra rab rnams kyang mthong ba ma yin
[\[34a\]]
[\[34a.1\]]pas/_/du ma'i gzugs su min pa'ang de dang 'dra/_/rdul phran cha shas med pa nyid kyang ni/_/phra rab du ma 'dus pa yin min pas/_/sa yi dkyil 'khor la sogs rang bzhin te/_/bsags pa 'ga' yang 'dir ni med par 'gyur/_/de bas 'dzin po la sogs
[\[34a.2\]]dang bral bas/_/rang rgyud gzugs sogs brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid/_/rgyu dang mi rgyu dngos po ma lus pa/_/dri za'i grong khyer dag dang mtshungs pa yin/_/bdag dang bdag gi rnam rtog rgyun gyi ni/_/ngo bo bdag gis der ni 'khor ba ste/_/dag pa phyin ci log de med pa yi/_/ngo bo tsam gyis rnam par shes
[\[34a.3\]]par bya/_/'dir ni zhi dang srid pa'i ngo bo dag_/chos nyid kyis ni dbye ba 'ga' yang med/_/gang phyir gzung ba la sogs rnam pa dang /_/bral bar thams cad du ni rtag tu grub/_/de ni snang ba'i rang bzhin kun rtog las/_/thams cad ci yang yod pa ma yin te/_/sems las gzhan pa dag ces bya ba ni/_/yod
[\[34a.4\]]pa ma yin de phyir de bdag nyid/_/gang zhig gzugs la so sor zhugs gyur pa/_/de yi bdag nyid gang yin de nyid gzugs/_/de bas thams cad khyad par med par brtag_/snang bar gyur pa'i yul rnams gang yin pa/_/gang zhig rtog pa'i gnas su gyur pa rnams/_/de de gnyis su sbyor ba dang bral bas/_/
[\[34a.5\]]des na rnam par dbye ba thams cad min/_/dad dang brtson 'grus rnam par dag pa dang /_/de bzhin dran dang bsam gtan rnam dag ba'ang /_/sgo bzangs srung bar byed pa'i ngo bo nyid/_/shes rab rnam dag ma lus yul du snang /_/mtshan ma med pa'i dga' ba rnam dag pa/_/ma lus lha mo'i tshogs kyi ngo bo nyid/_/
[\[34a.6\]]sems can don dang bdag dang rnam rtog dang /_/'jug pa'i rnam shes rnam par dag pa yang /_/me long sogs yid dri med ngo bo bas/_/sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yang rang bzhin te/_/de bzhin nyid ni rnam dag sbyor ba yis/_/'khor lo'i gtso bo 'di ni rnam par bzhugs/_/gzugs la sogs
[\[34a.7\]]pa'i 'khrul pa rnam bral bas/_/dri med phung po la sogs ngo bor grub/_/ser sna la sogs ldog par gyur ba ni/_/pha rol phyin pa dkar po'i chos rang bzhin/_/rnam rtog med par bdag gzhan don 'byung ba'i/_/rgyu nyid kyis ni de yang go rims bzhin/_/zab pa dang ni rgya che ba yis na/_/shes rab
[\[34b\]]
[\[34b.1\]]thabs kyi bdag nyid can sems yin/_/dam pa'i don du ci yang gzhan dag las/_/dbye med dbye ba med min mi 'dod de/_/gzhan du 'dzin pa las ni bzlog phyir dang /_/de bzhin bye brag la sogs rtog bral yin/_/de ltar brtags nas rang snying dri med pa/_/zla ba la gnas mtshan mar bsgom par
[\[34b.2\]]bya/_/gsang sngags dam pa thig le'i gzugs su ni/_/rang yid 'od dang ldan par yongs su bsgom/_/sems de'i 'od zer dri med pas sad pa'i/_/sku gsung rdo rje'i lus ni mchog gyur pa'i/_/slar yang 'di nyid du ni nges bzhugs shing /_/ye shes bdud rtsi 'bab par bsam par bya/_/nang gi
[\[34b.3\]]lus dang de bzhin thams cad kyang /_/de yis kun du mthar ni snang byas nas/_/ba spu re re'i khong las byung ba yi/_/'od kyis sna tshogs kun du dgang bar bya/_/yang na rang gi mtshan ma phra mo ni/_/'od ldan sna rtser gnas par thub pa yi/_/'khor lo nang du chud byas snying rje yis/_/nang gi shes rab dam
[\[34b.4\]]pa nyin mtshan bsgom/_/mtshan ma brtan po mthong na spro ba ni/_/'od zer de yis sprul pa'i thub dbang dang /_/rnam pa sna tshogs pa yi phyag mtshan rnams/_/blo dang ldan pas yang dang yang du spro/_/yang na bzlas la rtse gcig sems nyid ni/_/dngos kun bdag nyid rang gi sems dbang po/_/rang gi sngags
[\[34b.5\]]ni sna tshogs 'od ldan par/_/byas pas blo dang ldan pas bsgom par bya/_/srog dang rtsol ba shin tu ma bsdams par/_/gsang sngags rgyal po gsal bar brjod bya zhing /_/sku sogs rim pa bzhin du yang na ni/_/cig car spro ba dag ni legs par bya/_/nam mkha'i gtos dang mnyam pa sku sogs
[\[34b.6\]]pa'i/_/'od kyi sku yi snang bas yang dag dgang /_/de nas snga ma bzhin du sna tshogs pa'i/_/mchod pa'i sprin gyi bkod pa kun du spro/_/yongs su sbas pa'i rig pa mchog rnams ni/_/bde chen babs pas gzhan gyi dbang thob nas/_/rnam par sgeg pa'i thub dbang tshogs rnams ni/_/mthar ni rang
[\[34b.7\]]gi lus la gzhug par bya/_/rang gi snying po'i de nyid nges rtogs pa'i/_/skyo bas sems kyi spyod pa zhum gyur na/_/rig pa'i tshogs kyis yang dag glur blangs pas/_/rab tu bskul nas yongs su mchod par bya/_/sems bzang po yi chu rgyun srog dang ni/_/rtsol ba'i 'od kyi lcags kyus drangs
[\[35a\]]
[\[35a.1\]]nas ni/_/cho ga ji bzhin sku rdo rje sogs la/_/nges par dbab pas skyo ba bsal bar bya/_/de ltar thang cig ngal bso byas nas ni/_/sngar bshad cho ga yis ni de nyid shes/_/gsang sngags dam pa rgyun du bzla ba ni/_/sngags pa'ang kun du chags pa med par bya/_/bstod dang mchod
[\[35a.2\]]sogs gshegs su gsol ba dang /_/sngags pas rab tu 'bad de rnams bya zhing /_/oM la sogs par 'khor lo bsdus nas ni/_/sku la sogs pa brtag pa dag tu bya/_/de ltar de nyid mthong bas rnam grol ba/_/sems can khams rnams kun du dmigs nas ni/_/snying rjes 'gro ba rnams la phan don
[\[35a.3\]]du/_/smon lam rnams ni mngon sum nyid du bya/_/langs nas dag pa'i sems dpa' rang gi lha'i/_/rnam pa'i nga rgyal yid la byas nas ni/_/kun du snang bar gnas pa'i yul rnams ni/_/snga ma bzhin du yul du yongs su bsgom/_/rang rang gi ni ngo bo rnam dag pa/_/rim bzhin sku la sogs pa'i rdo rjer
[\[35a.4\]]gyur/_/dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa lta bur ni/_/chos nyid kyis na phan tshun khyad par med/_/phyin ci log gi rtog pa spangs pa yis/_/bya ba ma lus pa ni rdzogs par bya/_/de yi thub pa'i 'khor lo ma lus pa/_/mchod pa 'di ni kun du mchog yin no/_/bza' za'i tshe na snying ga'i zla ba la/_/'khor lo'i
[\[35a.5\]]gtso bo rang gi gsang sngags kyis/_/kun du dmigs te byang chub sems kyis ni/_/ngo bo nyid gyur 'od dang ldan par bsam/_/rang gi zas la de nyid gsum bzlas te/_/thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyis rnam dag pa/_/de yis sku yi rdo rje la sogs pa/_/lha rnams kun du tshim pa nyid du bya/_/phyi yi
[\[35a.6\]]sbyin sreg cho gas bsgre bya zhing /_/yid kyi'ang yid nyid kyis ni bya ba ste/_/phung po'i bud shing rnam par bsreg pa yi/_/ye shes 'bar ba bla na med par bshad/_/de ltar ma lus pa yi 'dod pa yis/_/bdag nyid dam ni gzhan dag rang rang gi/_/lha yi gzugs gyur pa la yang dag mchod/_/dam
[\[35a.7\]]tshig 'di ni bde gshegs rnams kyis gnang /_/rjes su mthun pa'i 'gro ba'i don rnams ni/_/ma lus bde gshegs mchod par yang dag brtag_/lus la sogs pa'i las rnams de dang de/_/rtag tu legs par mnyam par gzhag ste bya/_/rnam pa de 'dra'i sems ldan lus dang ni/_/ngag yid
[\[35b\]]
[\[35b.1\]]las rnams ci yang rung ba dag_/phyag rgya dang ni sngags kyi rnam pa ru/_/rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kun gyis de gsungs so/_/gang phyir dngos po gcig la'ang sna tshogs pa'i/_/kun du rtog pas bsags pa'i rnam pa las/_/sdug bsngal bde dang grol ba skyed byed pa'i/_/las kyi khyad par
[\[35b.2\]]mang po 'byung bar 'gyur/_/de bas lus sogs dge dang mi dge ba'i/_/rnam pa'i las rnams sems kyi dbang las gsungs/_/de ltar rnyog pa ma lus spangs pa yi/_/sems ni nag po'i las su ga la 'gyur/_/dam tshig nyams la snying ga'i zla bar ni/_/snying pos sna tshogs rdo rje ji bzhin
[\[35b.3\]]bsam/_/dpal ldan dam tshig rdo rje'i rnal 'byor pas/_/'gro ba rang bzhin gyis dag rnam bsams la/_/sna tshogs pad+ma'i 'dab ma'i dbus su ni/_/sngar gyi rim pas dbang bskur kun du blang /_/phyi rol gyi yang khrus kyi cho ga la/_/rim 'di khyad par du yang bsam par bya/_/thun mtshams su yang
[\[35b.4\]]de bzhin mchod la sogs/_/sngon du 'gro ba'i bzlas brjod byas nas ni/_/snying ga'i nang du 'khor lo chud byas la/_/snying rje dang ni shes rab ldan par nyal/_/ldang ba'i dus su dam tshig lha mo yi/_/yang dag glu yis dpal ldan bskul pas ni/_/langs na thub pas bzlas brjod la sogs
[\[35b.5\]]pa/_/cho ga snga ma bzhin du bya ba yin/_/dngos grub thob pa'i mtshan ma mthong nas ni/_/de nyid gsum mchod byas nas rang gi sems/_/sngar bshad dkyil 'khor dag la gnas nas ni/_/'dod pa'i dngos grub rab tu bsgrub par bya/_/bgegs rnams bdud rtsi thab sbyor 'khor lo yis/_/dbang
[\[35b.6\]]bskur byas nas 'bad pa med par 'joms/_/gang zhig dbus su gnas par gyur pa yis/_/'khor lo de yang de yi yin par 'gyur/_/tha mal rnam rtog rgyun las gzhan pa yi/_/srid pa'i sdug bsngal gzhan ci'ang yod ma yin/_/de dang rnam par 'gal bar 'gyur ba'i sems/_/'di ni mngon
[\[35b.7\]]sum du ni rtogs par 'gyur/_/zab cing rgya che ba yi bdag nyid can/_/gang yin der ni kun rtog snang mi 'gyur/_/rig pa las ni gzhan du gyur pa dag_/yod pa min par sngar ni bsgrubs pas na/_/gang zhig gang dang mi mthun pa dag tu/_/lan cig gyur pa'ang de bgrod rgyas gyur pa/_/mthong ba'i
[\[36a\]]
[\[36a.1\]]bslab pa rnam par 'phel ba yis/_/rang gi mi mthun shin tu 'gag par byed/_/sbyin pa la sogs bdag med ldan pas kyang /_/tha mal pa yi rang gi ngo bo las/_/rnam par ldog par mi 'gyur gang phyir 'dir/_/yod kyang de ni mi mthun 'gyur ma yin/_/de ltar rtogs na snying rjer
[\[36a.2\]]ldan pa dag_/ye shes bsam yas skad cig gis sgrub pa/_/dpal ldan kun du bzang po'i rang gi ni/_/ngo bo su zhig nges par sgom mi byed/_/dri med blo yi 'od zer rnams kyis ni/_/mun pa thams cad rnam par sel byed pa/_/rnam par bstan pas mdzad pa 'dis mchog gi/_/bdag 'dra'i go skabs dag ni
[\[36a.3\]]ga la yod/_/bla ma dam pa'i gzhung ni cung zad tsam/_/bzung ba gang yin de yang dang por ni/_/'ching ba lhod ces bya bar grags pas na/_/des na 'di la shin tu 'bad pa yin/_/de ltar rnam par sbyar las legs byung ba'i/_/dge ba dri med gang des 'gro ba'i yid/_/sangs rgyas ye shes mgon dang
[\[36a.4\]]bcas pa der/_/gzhol bar gyur pas rtag tu bsgom par shog_/dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i sgrub pa'i thabs kun du bzang po zhes bya ba/_byang chub sems dpa' 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhabs kyi pad+ma'i ze'u 'bru'i rdul la reg pa/_slob dpon chen po sangs rgyas ye shes kyi zhal snga nas kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//_//_
[\[36a.5\]]paN+Di ta shrad+d+hA kar warma dang /_lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o//[ {D1856}]@#/_/rgya gar skad du/_tsa tu rAM ga sA d+ha nAM no pi ka sa man+ta b+ha drI nA ma/bod skad du/_yan lag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs kun du bzang mo zhes bya ba/_dpal rdo rje sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal lo/_/dpal ldan 'khrul pa kun bsal dri ma med pa yi/_/gzi brjid
[\[36a.6\]]mtha' yas rigs kyi sprul pas rnam brgyan pa/_/shes rab ma yis lus 'khyud mdzes pas klubs pa gang /_/'jam dpal de la de mchod don dngos cho ga 'di bshad bya/_/dpal ldan 'dus pa'i tshul gyis dam pa'i bshes gnyen gsol gdab byed brod pas/_/'gro ba'i don kun phun sum tshogs
[\[36a.7\]]gzhi dngos po cho ga bshad par bya/_/skabs ldan g.yo ba 'di dang dam pa'i skye bo dang 'grogs shin tu thob dka' 'jig rten la/_/de phyir thabs dang shes rab mthar phyin byed 'dod sems ni mchog tu gyur pa yin/_/de nas snying rje'i mthu las byung ba'i byang chub yid ldan gsang sngags pa/_/gtong ba
[\[36b\]]
[\[36b.1\]]la sogs yon tan brgyad pa zab mo'i tshul la mos pa'am/_/dpal ldan gsang 'dus dkyil 'khor cho gas shin tu dbang bskur phun sum ldan/_/cho ga bzhin du lung stsal thob pa bzhi sngags bsnyen pa blo ldan pas/_/gang zhig dri med chu sogs ljon shing mchog gi phreng ba klubs pa yi/_/goms
[\[36b.2\]]pa'i ri la bcom ldan 'jam dbyangs zhes bya rab tu bsgrub par bya/_/dang po tho rangs snying ga'i dbus su dri med 'od 'phro de nyid bsam/_/bkod nas snying rje can gyis sgo la sogs pa yang dag par yang bya/_/dam pa'i tsan+dan sogs bkrus dri zhim me tog bkram pa'i mchog cha la/_/bsam gtan gnas
[\[36b.3\]]su bde ba'i gnas su 'dug nas dus gsum sangs rgyas rnams/_/dmigs te sna tshogs mchod sprin spro sogs sngon du byas nas blo ldan pas/_/sdig pa la sogs 'di ltar bya'o dge ba 'phel don du/_/thog ma med ldan srid pa'i rgyun la rtog pas bsags pa'i sdig kun gang /_/snying rje chen po'i mdun
[\[36b.4\]]rim bzhin te thams cad bshags par bgyi/_/yang dag sangs rgyas byang chub 'phags dang gzhan rnams mdzad pa'i dge ba gang /_/ma lus bdag gis yi rang yang dag de ni byang chub phyir bsngo'o/_/sems rgyas zla ba dri ma med las grub pas mtha' yas snying rje gnas/_/bdag gi yid la gnas
[\[36b.5\]]pa'i bde bar gshegs la rtag tu skyabs su mchi/_/rtog pa kun las nges grol ma lus dam pa sems dpa'i bkra shis gzhi/_/dngos po kun gyi ngo bor chos la bdag nyid skyabs su mchi/_/bcings pas yang dag spangs pa'i snying rje mchog gis drangs pa'i dpal ldan pa/_/rab dga' la sogs sa la gnas
[\[36b.6\]]pa dam bcas tshogs la skyabs su mchi/_/bsam pa rnam smin dag pas sgrib kun bag chags ma lus bcom pa ste/_/mos pas rnam par brgyan pa'i sems kyis byang chub sems ni bskyed par bgyi/_/bde gshegs sras bcas lam gcig sbyin sogs bcu po dkar po yon tan ngo bo la/_/rdzogs
[\[36b.7\]]sangs rgyas dag kun gyi rang bzhin blo yis de ltar bsten par bgyi/_/'jig rten 'di dag lta ba'i dra bas bkab la snying rjes dmigs nas su/_/yang dag byang chub sems kyi gzhal med bsgom rim 'di ni sngags pas bya/_/stong pa rang bzhin med phyir rgyu 'bras phyir ni rang bzhin mtshan ma med/_/rjes
[\[37a\]]
[\[37a.1\]]su dpag pa bsal bas ma lus gzhi yi smon pa nges bral lo/_/oM shU n+ya tA dz+nyA na badzra swa b+hA wa At+ma ko\u0f85haM/_de 'og ston zla dkar po mtha' med phyogs 'khor gnas pa sna tshogs 'od/_/'phags par gnas pa'i gru gsum nang gi mkha' yi rang bzhin rdo rje 'dzin/_/chos kyi
[\[37a.2\]]'byung zhes phyag rgya dbus gnas pad+ma sna tshogs rdo rjes brgyan/_/hUM gis rdo rje brgyan pa'i sa la kun du bzang po las byung bsgom/_/b+h+rUM yig 'khor lo las byung rig ma dang bcas snang mdzad skur gyur pa/_/gsal ba thub dbang dkyil 'khor sna tshogs 'od zer gyis khyab phyogs 'khor kun/_/gru bzhi mnyam
[\[37a.3\]]pa'i phyir na mchog bzhis dran pa dbang po sgo rnams kyis/_/bsam gtan bzhi yi twar Na ting 'dzin mu khyud bzhi yis yongs bskor ba/_/mu khyud de la gnas pa dam pa'i mchod pas 'brel ba'i gzugs rnams rgyun/_/sna tshogs rgyan rnams bkod pa 'gro ba'i bsam pa thams cad yongs rdzogs
[\[37a.4\]]phyir/_/'dul bas bskyod pa gsung rab yan lag dgu yi dam chos kun 'gro ci yi phyir/_/rlung gis bskyod pa rgyal mtshan phreng dang dril sgra grag pas phyogs sgo kun/_/me long ye shes rtag tu dri med byang chub yan lag me tog spos bkram zhing /_/dra ba dra phyed me long me tog phreng ba sna tshogs brgyan
[\[37a.5\]]pa'i gzugs/_/rnam par thar brgyad rnam par dag pas ka ba brgyad kyis klubs pa'i mchog_/rdo rje tshul gyis chos kyi 'khor los sgyur phyir rdo rje'i thig ldan la/_/gzugs la sogs pa'i spyod yul dag pas bla med mtha' yas 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga/_/zas lngas brgyan pas rnam par dag pa'i chos kyi
[\[37a.6\]]dbyings rgyu mthun/_/sna tshogs pad+ma la gnas nyi ma zla bar bcas pa lha yi gdan/_/ma lus rin chen bkod pa'i gzhal yas brtsegs pa de la bsgom/_/bcu drug cha shas sde pa las byung zla ba'i dkyil 'khor ba yi dbus/_/dbus kyi gdan la cho ga bzhin du 'od dpag med gzhi bsam par bya/_/mchog
[\[37a.7\]]gi dang po'i snying po las byung rdo rje dam pa ye shes gzugs/_/grangs med thug pa'i 'od zer phreng bas grub pa'i phyogs sgo kun/_/bsams nas dang po'i snying por bcas pa'i nga rgyal ldan pas sprul pa mtha' yas kyis/_/'gro ba'i don mchog rab mdzad pa yi thugs mchog rdul phran rnam bkod gzugs
[\[37b\]]
[\[37b.1\]]brnyan can/_/g.yas g.yon zhal ni gnag dang dmar po zla ba rdzogs ltar dkar ba'i mdog_/gsal bas rnam par bkod pas brgyan pa'i phyag gnyis dam pa'i rig ma 'khyud/_/lhag ma'i phyag zung gnyis brgyan rdo rje ral gri rin chen pad+ma 'dzin/_/'jig rten gsum khong brgyan pa'i 'od zer rnam
[\[37b.2\]]pa bde 'gro thub pa'i dbang /_/rnam thar gsum dag shes rab bdag nyid snying rje'i mchog gi thabs ldan pas/_/'gro kun de nyid gcig pa rgyal ba skyed byed sku bzhi mngon sum bya/_/mchog tu rjes chags phun sum tshogs pas 'jig rten thams cad 'dul dmigs nas/_/dga' ba'i rdzu 'phrul
[\[37b.3\]]sgra yis rgyal ba'i tshogs rnams rang gi lus nang bzhugs/_/de ni spyan la sogs pa'i lha mo gzugs sogs yul gyi rang bzhin pas/_/phyung nas rig ma thams cad gzhi yi rig ma'i nang du thim par bya/_/de yi pad+ma'i snying po'i dbus su dkyil 'khor dri med zla 'od las byung ba/_/blo yis bsams
[\[37b.4\]]nas rdzogs par bde la skye bo'i tshogs rnams gzhug par bya/_/dam pa gsang ba'i rdo rje dkyil 'khor rnam snang mdzad sogs rgyal ba'i rgyan zhugs nas/_/zla ba zhu ba'i ngo bor gyur pas dbang bskur byas te de 'og tu/_/sa snying phyag na rdo rje nam snying 'jig rten dbang phyug sgrib pa sel/_/dpal ldan
[\[37b.5\]]kun du bzang po de dag mig la sogs pa'i grangs su gyur/_/gzugs sgra dri dang ro dang reg bya chos dbyings rdo rje yang /_/sa chu me rlung rang bzhin gyur pa spyan la sogs pa'i grangs 'gyur ro/_/gzugs dang myong ba mtshan ma de bzhin kho na 'du byed yid brjod pas/_/rnam snang mdzad sogs bde gshegs
[\[37b.6\]]rnams te de 'og sa bon gyis dbyung bya/_/k+ShiM dzr-IM khaM gaM Sh+kaM saM brjod pa de dag mig la sogs rnams so/_/myong ba mtshan ma de bzhin kho na 'du byed yid brjod pa/_/rnam snang mdzad sogs bde gshegs dzaH hUM baM hoH khaM raM brjod pas gzugs kyi rdo rje la sogs so/_/laM mAM paM tAM zhes kyang gsungs pa de
[\[37b.7\]]bzhin spyan la sogs pa'o/_/b+h+rUM AM dzr-IM hUM zhes pas rtag pa la sogs so/_/oM AH hUM zhes sems 'bar ho yi bar du zhugs pa cho ga bzhin/_/pad+ma'i nang gnas mnyam med shes rab chags pas zhu ba byed mthong ste/_/de yi 'od kyi mthu yis kyang ni zla ba zhu bar byed mthong ste/_/'di ltar spyan la
[\[38a\]]
[\[38a.1\]]sogs pa'i lha mo'i dbyangs kyi sgra yis bskul bar bsam/_sems can khams na gnas pa'i dbang phyug khyod ni rdo rje'i thugs/_/dga' ba yid 'ong don chen 'dod pas bdag la bskyab tu gsol/_/mgon po gal te de ring bdag ni gson par mchis bzhed na/_/sems
[\[38a.2\]]can yab chen gnyen mchog bdag la dgyes par mdzad du gsol/_/rdo rje'i sku khyod bka' yi 'khor los sems can kun la phan/_/sangs rgyas don du byang chub mchog sgrub rab tu phan par gzigs/_/mgon po gal te bdag ni de ring gson par mchis bzhed na/_/'dod chags dam tshig chags
[\[38a.3\]]pas bdag la dgyes par mdzad du gsol/_/khyod ni rdo rje'i gsung ste kun la phan pa'i thugs brtse ba/_/'jig rten dag gi dgongs pa'i don mdzad pa la rtag tu brtson/_/mgon po gal te bdag ni de ring gson par mchis bzhed na/_/spyod pa dri med kun du bzang pos bdag la dgyes par mdzod/_/
[\[38a.4\]]khyod ni rdo rje'i 'dod pa dam tshig mchog gi phan don che/_/yang dag rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi gdung mchog mnyam pa nyid gzigs pa/_/mgon po gal te bdag ni de ring gson par mchis bzhed na/_/yon tan rin chen mang po'i gter gyur bdag la dgyes par mdzod/_/de ltar dbyangs kyis bskul
[\[38a.5\]]bas sgyu 'phrul dra bar dngos kun legs bsams nas/_/'od zer 'bar bas bskor ba'i gzhi yi sngags kyis lus su rang bsgyur bya/_/de la 'od kyis ma lus lha rnams rgyal ba'i thub dbang rnams/_/nang du thim nas 'od kyis dpal ldan 'jam pa'i rdo rjer gyur par bya/_/gur kum mchog 'od dmar
[\[38a.6\]]'dra g.yas g.yon zhal ni gnag dang dkar ba'i mdog_/sna tshogs rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i phyag gnyis dam pa'i shes rab 'khyud/_/gsal ba'i ral gri mda' dang ut+pal mthing ga gzhu ni mtha' yas 'od/_/ma lus rigs rnams 'phro bas brgyan pa'i mkha' kun dkyil 'khor ldan skyob pa/_/gzung
[\[38a.7\]]'dzin bral bas dngos po thams cad ngo bo nyid med shes nas su/_/rnam par byang ba mngon bzhugs zab don byin brlabs 'di ltar bya/_/oM d+harma d+hA tu swa b+hA wa At+ma ko\u0f85haM/_/de 'og gzhi yi sa bon 'od kyis ji ltar rang la gang ste mig sogs rnams/_/sa snying la sogs dri med rang snying zla ba'i rdo rje bum
[\[38b\]]
[\[38b.1\]]pa'i dkyil gnas pa/_/hUM gi thugs kyi rdo rje kha dang mgo la pad+ma 'khor lo'i dkyil du yang /_/AH dang phyag mtshan gnyis kyis gsung gi rdo rje sku yi rdo rje'ang bsam par bya/_/de thugs 'od zer rgyun gyis rang gi shes rab dang sbyor snang bas kun du ni/_/rgyal ba'i dbang po rnams la mchod nas thugs
[\[38b.2\]]kyi rdo rje la sogs byin gyis brlab/_/dpal ldan thugs kyi rdo rje 'chang /_/rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms pas/_/de ring bdag la byin brlabs nas/_/thugs kyi rdo rjes mdzad du gsol/_/phyogs bcur bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams/_/rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms nas/_/de ring bdag
[\[38b.3\]]la byin brlabs nas/_/thugs kyi rdo rjes mdzad du gsol/_/oM sarba ta thA ga ta tsit+ta badzra swa b+hA wa At+ma ko\u0f85haM/_dpal ldan chos kyi gsung gi lam/_/rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms pas/_/de ring bdag la byin brlabs nas/_/gsung gi rdo rjes mdzad du gsol/_/phyogs bcur bzhugs
[\[38b.4\]]pa'i sangs rgyas rnams/_/rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms pas/_/de ring bdag la byin brlabs nas/_/gsung gi rdo rjes mdzad du gsol/_/oM sarba ta thA ga ta wA ka badzra swa b+hA wa At+ma ko\u0f85haM/_dpal ldan sku yi rdo rje 'chang /_/rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms pas/_/de ring bdag la byin brlabs
[\[38b.5\]]nas/_/sku yi rdo rjes mdzad du gsol/_/phyogs bcur bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams/_/rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms pas/_/de ring bdag la byin brlabs nas/_/sku yi rdo rjes mdzad du gsol/_/oM sarba ta thA ga ta kA ya badzra swa b+hA wa At+ma ko\u0f85haM/_rdo rje gsum ni nam mkha'i rang bzhin
[\[38b.6\]]mtshan ma spangs pa mtshon byas te/_/sems kyi 'od zer rnams kyis bskul nas thams cad tshogs su gyur pa'i thub pa'i sde/_/thub mchog 'od zer las byung rig ma'i tshogs kyis yang dag 'dzin pa yi/_/bum pa'i ye shes chu yis blugs pas rang rig gtso bo snang bas dbu brgyan gyur/_/
[\[38b.7\]]de bzhin rang gi lha mo 'dra bar rang gi snying po'ang bsgoms nas rig mar sprul/_/mig la sogs pa gang nas yig 'bru gsum bkod 'bar ba'i lus ldan ma/_/'og snying lte ba gsang ba de bzhin brla gnyis sogs la de nyid shes par bya/_/oM hUM swA AH hA zhes bya bas lus yid rdo rje dam pa'i
[\[39a\]]
[\[39a.1\]]rigs tshogs kyi/_/de lnga'i byin rlabs lus ni 'gro gsum khyab pas dam pa'i 'od tshogs bsam/_/AH sa bskyed rnam par bkod pa'i snying po hUM las sprul pa'i pad+ma 'dab brgyad pa/_/pad+ma'i shes rab rgyu mthun rang bzhin thabs dang bcas par gyur pa'i gzhi yi lus
[\[39a.2\]]bsngags pa/_/de dang lhan cig bde gshegs rnams la rjes su chags par bgyi zhes brtsams/_/oM sarba ta thA ga tA nu rA ga na badzra swa b+hA wa At+ma ko\u0f85haM/_/sems kyi zla ba'i 'od kyis ma lus sangs rgyas tshogs ni bzhugs gnas te/_/hUM gi rdo rjer byung nas dri med pad+ma la gnas dam pa'i yid kyi
[\[39a.3\]]gzugs/_/bsams nas rang gi snying pos bskyed pa thams cad gzhi yi dkyil 'khor lha gzugs su/_/mchog gi rjes su dkar mo zhes par mtha' yas yon tan rin chen ma/_/rin chen dbang phyug dra ba'i dngos po sgrol ba badzra ra tI zhes bskul bas/_/dri med rin chen phreng bas bsgoms pa'i phyogs
[\[39a.4\]]'khor byed ma dbang ldan la/_/dam pa'i 'khor lo ut+pal dmar po pad+ma ut+pal ser po rnams kyis mtshan/_/de dag gi ni rim pa'i nges pa'i lhag ma'i ji ltar 'dod pa'i phyag bsnams yin/_/dkyil 'khor grwa bzhi dang ni shar gyi sgo gnyis la ni bsam bya ba/_/gzugs sogs rdo rje lha mo sku la sogs dang gsum
[\[39a.5\]]gyis so/_/shar gyi sgo ru grags pa bsam pa thams cad 'grub mtha' yas pas 'jigs pa'i 'od/_/'bar la ya mAn+ta kr-ita ces bas zad dus drag sprin dkyil 'khor dngos po ste/_/thugs bdag rgyal po mnyam pa'i sku ni du ma'i khro bo rigs kyi 'od phyung ba/_/gshin rje mthar byed ces bya mi bzad
[\[39a.6\]]pa yi sbrul gyis sku brgyan dpal ldan pa'o/_/lho phyogs kyi sgor gnas pa pradz+nyAn+ta kr-ita ces pas bla na med ldan pa/_/sku yi dbang phyug bzhin du phyag la sogs pa drag po gzhan gyis mi thub gsal/_/de nas rta mgrin nub kyi phyogs su sgo ru 'od zer 'khrigs pas phyogs bskor ba/_/pad+mAn+ta kr-ita ces pas
[\[39a.7\]]'bar ba'i 'jig pa'i me ltar 'jigs pa'i gzugs/_/gsung gi bzhin du phyag la sogs pa du mas sdang ba 'jigs byed zhal/_/gad sgrogs bzhad pas ri rnams g.yo bar byed dang thub pa'i dbang rnams so/_/de nas mi bskyod 'dra ba'i zhal sogs big+h+nAn+ta kr-ita ces bya byang sgo ru/_/zad dus byin za lta bu
[\[39b\]]
[\[39b.1\]]'phags pa bdud rtsi 'khyil pa dpa' ba'o/_/rnam snang mdzad dang thub dbang snang ba mtha' yas thugs kyi dbang phyug dbu rgyan dang /_/rim par tho ba be con pad+ma rdo rje la sogs phyag kyang de bzhin no/_/de ltar rdzogs par bskyed par dkyil 'khor mthong nas dngos po thams cad kyis/_/snying po sngags
[\[39b.2\]]kyi 'od zer lcags kyus bde gshegs spyan drangs bsgom par bya/_/thabs dang shes rab dngos po dri med ting 'dzin las byung dam pa'i bde bas gsang bar ni/_/dkyil 'khor bsams te de nas mthar byed la sogs bsrung byas nas/_/rang snying bzlas pa'i tsan+dan sogs dang me tog mdzes pa phul
[\[39b.3\]]te thim/_/rang dang 'dra ba'i cho gas dbang bskur byas nas 'di ltar nan tan mchod par bya/_/pad+ma'i nang gi rang gi sa bon 'od kyis drangs nas gzugs sogs thams cad ni/_/pad+ma'i 'od zer dkyil 'khor yang dag byang chub yid kyi sa bon bsam par bya/_/shes rab so so'i ba spu'i las byung sna tshogs
[\[39b.4\]]rnam pa'i 'od zer rgyas pa'i tshogs/_/ma lus khyab pa'i mkha' gzhi thams cad de nas blo dang ldan pas spro bar bya/_/'od zer sgo nas byung ba'i dri med thams cad rgyan gyis shin tu brgyan sku dang /_/me long pi wang dri dang ro yi snod dang na bza' chos 'byung la sogs dang /_/mtshan ma rnams kyi rim pas
[\[39b.5\]]mdzes pas ldem bag phyag ni lo ma 'od dang bcas/_/gsal ba'i 'od zer sprul pa mang po sna tshogs mchod pa'i sprin gyi dra ba rnams 'byung dang /_/sgyu ma la sogs dra ba'i dngos po so so yang dag rig pa'i 'jig rten lta dge dang /_/rtog pa thams cad nges grol mchog gi bde ba 'byung rgyu'i dngos ldan pa'i/_/
[\[39b.6\]]gzugs la sogs pa'i lha mo rnams kyis de bzhin phyi ma'i dri sogs thams cad kyis/_/dbye ba'i rtog pa grol bas rgyal ba'i dbang po rnams la yang dag mchod par bya/_/oM sarba ta thA ga ta pU dza badzra swa b+hA wa At+ma ko\u0f85haM/_de yi 'og tu sgra brnyan 'dra bar sgra yul thams cad la ni yod bsams na/_/rang yid
[\[39b.7\]]rig pa'i lha yi stod pa'i sgra dang ldan pa'i chos rnams zhes su gsungs/_/gzugs la sogs pa gcig min rdul phran cha yang ma mthong du ma'i gzugs kyang ma yin zhes pa'ang de bzhin no/_/yan lag med pa'i rdul phran nyid la du ma'i rdul phra rab kyi rjes 'brang med phyir dang /_/sa yi dkyil 'khor la_
[\[40a\]]
[\[40a.1\]]sogs gzugs kyi dbye bas de la 'ga' yang mi 'gyur ro/_/de bas 'dzin pa la sogs bral bas rang dbang gzugs la sogs pa kun brtags ngo bo yin/_/ma lus g.yo dang mi g.yo'i dngos po dri za'i grong khyer dag dang 'dra ba yin/_/bdag gir 'dzin pa'i rtog pa'i rgyun
[\[40a.2\]]gyi ngo bos 'khor ba 'di dag ste/_/dag pa yang ni de las ldog pa'i ngo bo tsam la rnam par shes par bya/_/chos nyid kyis ni srid dang zhi ba'i ngo bo 'dir ni dbye ba 'ga' yang med/_/ci'i phyir 'dzin pa la sogs rnam par bral ba rtag tu kun la sgrub pa'i phyir/_/thams cad 'ga' yang med de so sor snang ba'i
[\[40a.3\]]rang bzhin rtog pa las/_/sems las gzhan du gyur pa'i nga zhes 'ga' yang med de de phyir bdag kyang de/_/gang gi ngo bo gang yin de yis de nyid rtogs pa'i gzhi ste ci phyir dngos/_/de bas thams cad dbyer med shes te dngos po thams cad dbyer med pa nyid yin/_/kha cig yul dang kha cig gzhan du
[\[40a.4\]]snang bar rtogs pa phun sum tshogs pa gang zhig gis/_/de dang de yi bral dang bral ba'i phyis te de phyis thams cad ma yin no/_/dad dang brtson 'grus rnam par dag pa de bzhin dran pa bsam gtan dag pas kyang /_/dam pa'i sgo srung gzugs te shes rab rnam par dag pas thams cad yul du snang /_/mtshan
[\[40a.5\]]ma med pa'i dag pa thams cad dag pas lha mo tshogs kyi rang bzhin dang /_/thams cad don dang bdag po rnam par rtog pa rab tu 'jug pa rnam par dag pa yis/_/me long la sogs mkha' chen po/_/rdo rje gsum mchog dkyil 'khor gsum/_/rdo rje dbyangs la phyag 'tshal lo/_/rnam par snang
[\[40a.6\]]mdzad dag pa che/_/rdo rje zhi ba dga' ba che/_/rang bzhin gyis ni 'od gsal mchog_/ston pa rdo rje phyag 'tshal lo/_/rin chen rgyal po rab tu zab/_/rdo rje nam mkha' dri ma med/_/dngos nyid dag pas gos pa med/_/rdo rje sku la phyag 'tshal lo/_/rdo rje mi 'chi 'dod chags che/_/mi rtog nam mkha'i rdo rje
[\[40a.7\]]'dzin/_/'dod chags pha rol phyin pa brnyes/_/rdo rje gsung la phyag 'tshal lo/_/don yod rdo rje rdzogs sangs rgyas/_/bsam pa thams cad yongs rdzogs pa'i/_/dag pa ngo bo nyid las byung /_/rdo rje sems la phyag 'tshal lo/_/phyag 'tshal 'bar bas byin gyis brlabs pa'i rlung me'i dkyil
[\[40b\]]
[\[40b.1\]]'khor gnas 'bar ba'i/_/bdud rtsi lnga la de nas 'bru gsum bzlas pa'i dkyil nas grangs med thub pa'i dbang /_/ye shes bdud rtsi'i rang bzhin brtsams te yi ge hUM bkod rdo rje dam pa'i lce/_/snying ga'i zla ba'i dbus su ma lus rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor de yis tshim par bya/_/kun du 'khrul pa
[\[40b.2\]]spangs pa'i snying gi 'od zer las byung thub dbang mtha' yas kyi/_/'gro ba ma lus yang dag sangs rgyas byed pa bzhi yi sngags nang thim par bya/_/gzugs la sogs pa'i rnam par grol bas mngon sum gyis ni mthong min de 'dzin pa/_/gzung ba 'ga' yang med de gzhan yang yod pa ma yin 'brel
[\[40b.3\]]pa ma mthong bas/_/sim pa la sogs rang gi las kyang 'ga' yang ma mthong de yongs bzung bas na/_/dus gcig 'brel par gyur pa gzugs la sogs pa bzhin du de dag gzung 'dzin med/_/dkar po la sogs gang gis dang por mthong ba de nyid dus gzhan mthong ba min/_/de gnyis phan
[\[40b.4\]]tshun du yang mi mthun phyir na rtag tu sim la sogs pa bzhin/_/de nas bzlas pa byed 'dod sems kyis dngos kun bdag nyid rang sems bdag por ni/_/byas nas sems kyi 'od zer ldan pa bzhi yi sngags ni mkhas pas bsgom par bya/_/'phro bas sngags kyi rgyal po gsal bar gtong dang dgag pa'i
[\[40b.5\]]dbang du byas nas bzlas nas su/_/sku la sogs pa rnams kyi spro ba'i rim gyis sam ni dus gcig byas pa yis/_/nam mkha'i nang du sku la sogs pa'i 'od zer rnams kyis bkang bya ste/_/gong ma bzhin du sna tshogs mchod sprin tshogs rnams de nas kun du dbyung bar bya/_/mchog gi rig ma 'khyud pa bde
[\[40b.6\]]ba chen po chags pas gzhan dbang mthong nas su/_/rgyas pa thub pa'i dbang po'i rgyun ni rang gi lus la mthar ni thim par bya/_/gzhi yi snying po de nyid sems dpas lus nyams zhan pas sems kyi spyod chung ba/_/rig ma mchog gi dbyangs kyis rab tu gsol ba btab nas dkyil 'khor mchod par
[\[40b.7\]]bya'o/_/dam pa'i sems kyi chu rgyun 'gags pa'i dbugs kyi 'od zer lcags kyus drangs nas su/_/lus nyam chung na cho ga bzhin du sku yi rdo rje sogs la dbab par bya/_/de ltar skad cig 'dug nas gong nas gsungs pa'i cho ga yis ni de bzhin nyid shes pas/_/dam pa'i sngags kyis bzlas pa
[\[41a\]]
[\[41a.1\]]nyin mtshan med par bya'o sngags kyang ma 'dres pa'o/_/gsungs pa'i bstod dang mchod la sogs pa rdzogs par bskyed pa brtson pa'i sngags pa yis/_/phyag 'tshal la sogs bkod pa'i dkyil 'khor sku la sogs par rtog pa bsgom par bya'o/_/de 'dra'i cho ga
[\[41a.2\]]de nyid mthong bas sems can khams ni nges dgrol dmigs nas su/_/snying rjes 'gro la phan don brtan pa'i sems kyis cho ga 'di yis 'jig rten phan pa'i rgyu phyir 'byung bar bya/_/badzra d+h+r-ika ces bskul nas thugs kyi rdo rje 'gro ba'i don mchog byed pa ni/_/g.yas g.yon zhal ni dkar dmar 'bar
[\[41a.3\]]ba'i mthing ga dam pa nor bu 'dra ba'i mdog_/mchog gi dang po bzhin du phyag dang ldan pa du ma'i mdog gi 'od kyi tshogs/_/'dus nas bdag la blo dang ldan pas dngos po kun gyis thim par bya/_/dzi na dzika ces bskul ba'i rdo rje 'dzin ltar mdog dang zhal sogs ldan/_/shar gyi zla ba pad+ma'i dbus
[\[41a.4\]]su 'khor sogs mtshan pa de bzhin bsam/_/rat+na d+h+r-ika ces lho ru rin chen dbang phyug zhal rnams gzhon nu'i mdog 'dra ba/_/btso ma'i gser dang 'dra ba margad rin chen la sogs mdzes pa'i phyag drug pa/_/A ro l-i ka ces pad+ma rA ga bzhin du dmar la zhal gnyis de bzhin te/_/snang ba mtha' yas

[\[50a.1\]]brag ca dang ni gzugs brnyan dang /_/'khrul pa mgal me 'khor lo ru/_/skad cig sogs pas rab rtogs so/_/de bas thabs de dngos kun gyi/_/de nyid bden pas bsgrub pa'o/_/gnyis med bde ba gsang chen po'i/_/sangs rgyas byang chub sgrub byed pa/_/

[\[50b.1\]]bsregs sbyin sreg go/_/zab pa dang ni gsal ba yis/_/chos kun mnyam pas thig gdab po/_/gsal ba'i 'ja' tshon lta bu'i skus/_/nyi shu rtsa gcig chos kun la/_/rang bzhin gyis bzung mtshon btab po/_/de yi ngo bo kun gnas pa/_/slob dpon slob ma kun zhugs

[\[52a.1\]]bdag_/rdo rje 'chang ba kun gyi gnas/_/chos rnams kun gyi chos nyid de/_/sangs rgyas kun gyis bsgrub bya'o/_/sangs rgyas rnams kyis chos bstan pa/_/rim pa gnyis la yang dag gnas/_/bskyed pa yi ni rim nyid dang /_/rdzogs pa'i rim pa kho

[\[52a.7\]]bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//[ {D1860}]@#_/rgya gar skad du/_At+ma sA d+ha nA ba tA ra nA ma/_bod skad du/_bdag sgrub pa la 'jug pa zhes bya ba/_byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/_/dpal ldan rtog pa'i dri ma ma lus pa dang

[\[52b.1\]]bral zhing kun du rtog pa las/_/byung de'i bdag nyid 'gro ba thams cad nges par mi gnas sems ni gang yin 'dir/_/mdzes pa'i rnam pa'i yid rgyun cho gas lus can nges par legs pa'i gnas de la/_/phyag byas skye ba brgyud par nye bar 'tshe ba gcod byed yang dag bshad par bya/_/

[\[52b.4\]]yin nam ji ltar na rnam par rtog pa tsam gyi bdag nyid 'khor bar 'gyur zhe na/_ma yin te/_gzugs la sogs pa rtogs pa'i yul nyid du ma grub pa ste/_gzugs la sogs pa so sor snang ba ma rtogs par gzhan gzung ba'am/_de 'dzin pa cung zad kyang dmigs su med
[\[52b.5\]]pa'i phyir ro/_/yul rtogs par gyur pa ma yin par yang rang gi ngo bo yod pa'i tha snyad kyi yul mi 'grub ste/_shin tu thal bar 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/de dang 'brel pa'i dngos po gzhan rtogs pas de rtogs par 'gyur ba yang ma yin te/_'ga' zhig mngon sum gyi
[\[52b.6\]]bdag nyid las shin tu 'das pa la 'brel pa rab tu ma grub pa'i phyir ro/_/nang du so sor snang bar gyur pa rang gi bde ba la sogs pa'i snang ba ni 'dzin pa nyid yin la/_sngon po la sogs pa de las phyi rol gyi gzugs nyid du rtogs pa'i mtshan nyid ni gzung ba yin no zhe na ma yin te/_sngon
[\[52b.7\]]po la sogs pa la bde ba la sogs pa'i byed pa ma grub pa'i phyir ro/_/rtog pa'i byed pa med par yang 'dzin pa zhes bya ba de lta na ni/_phyi rol gyi gzugs la sogs pa yang 'dzin pa nyid du thal bar 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/cig car rang dbang nyid du so sor snang bdag ni/_cung zhig ni gzung
[\[53a\]]
[\[53a.1\]]ba/_cung zhig ni 'dzin pa'o zhes so sor nges pa'i rnam pa ni ma mthong ngo /_/bdag ni sngon po la sogs pa rig pa'o zhes bya ba yang rnam par rtog pa tsam nyid de/_phyi dang nang nyid du rang dgas so sor snang ba rnams khong du chud pa'i phyir ro/_/'dzin pa la sogs pa
[\[53a.2\]]rnam par rtog pa'i rgyun 'di thams cad nyid ni rang dbang du nyams su myong ba rab tu ston pa la gzhol ba yin te/_so sor snang ba rnams gcig la gcig yongs su 'dzin pa'i byed pa dang bral ba'i dngos po nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/de lta bas na 'ga' zhig la 'ga' zhig gis 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni ma
[\[53a.3\]]yin no/_/de ltar yang rab 'byor chos kyis chos yongs su shes pa ni ma yin no zhes bya ba rgyas par gsungs pa yin no/_/gang yang gzung ba ni shes pa gnyis kyis shes par byed do zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa de dang de ni gzugs la sogs pa zhen pa tsam la ltos nas la lar gang zag
[\[53a.4\]]la sogs pa bstan pa dang 'dra bas nyes pa med do/_/de lta yin du chug na yang 'gro ba rnams kyang rnam par rig pa tsam gyi rang bzhin gzung ba dang 'dzin pa med pa'i rang bzhin can yin la/_de yang ldog pa med pa'i phyir gang gis de rnam par ldog pa tsam mya ngan las 'das pa zhes bya zhe na/_ma yin
[\[53a.5\]]te rnam par shes pa yang gcig dang du ma'i rang bzhin dang bral ba yin pa'i phyir ro/_/'di ltar de gcig ma yin te/_/sngon po la sogs pa tha dad pas dmigs pa sna tshogs pa'i phyir ro/_/dkar po la sogs pa kha dog gcig pa yang thog ma dang dbus dang tha ma'i cha tha dad par snang ba'i phyir dang /_

[\[53a.7\]]te/_'di dag phan tshun med pa nyid pas 'gal ba'i phyir ro/_/thams cad du bdag med pa nyid ma yin nam gang dngos po rnams nyams su myong ba'i don byed pa'i rab tu dbye ba bya zhe na/_ma brtags gcig pu'i bdag nyid snga ma snga ma'i rnam par rtog pa tsam nyid yin pa'i phyir de rtogs pa las
[\[53b\]]
[\[53b.1\]]gzhan ma yin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya bas bstan to/_/de lta yin du chug na dngos po thams cad kyi ngo bo yod pa nyid du 'gyur te/_yod pa'i dngos po ni don byed nus pa'i mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir ro zhe na/_de ni ma yin te/_so sor snang ba tsam du yod par khas blangs pas mi 'gal ba yin pa'i

[\[53b.3\]]bzhin gyis stong pa nyid do zhes rgyas par gang gsungs pa yin no/_/de nyid kyi phyir kun rdzob kyi dngos po ma lus pa snga ma dang phyi ma'i dbye bas snang ba yin pa'i phyir/_rtag pa yin zhes dogs par mi bya'o/_/gang yang 'di lta ste/_kye rgyal ba'i sras khams gsum pa 'di dag ni rnam par
[\[53b.4\]]rig pa tsam mo zhes gsungs pa de yang shin tu dngos po la mngon par zhen pa dag phyi rol gyi don la zhen pa tsam bzlog pa'i phyir te/_de las ni bde ba la sogs pa sems tsam du zhen pa yang gsal ba srid pa'i phyir ro/_/de ltar yang /_sems tsam la ni brten nas su/_/phyi rol don la mi
[\[53b.5\]]brtag go/_/de bzhin nyid la dmigs nas ni/_/sems tsam las kyang 'da' bar bya/_/zhes gsungs pa yin no/_/de lta bas na 'di ltar nga dang nga'i zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i rnam par rtog pa'i rang bzhin can gyi 'gro ba'i skye ba de dang 'gal ba ni bshad ma thag pa'i rnam pas bdag med par
[\[53b.6\]]mthong ba yin pa'i phyir ro/_/phyin ci log gi gzhan gyi dbang du gyur pa'i 'gro ba de dag mngon par gdon pa'i phyir snying rje mchog gi bsam pa bskyed nas chos thams cad stong pa nyid kho na la dang por mngon du phyogs par bya'o/_/snying rjes rab tu phye ba yin yang gtong ba la sogs pa dmigs
[\[53b.7\]]pas rab tu phye ba'i sbyin pa la sogs pa'i dge ba'i rgyun ni bdag dang gzhan du rnam par rtog pa'i phyir/_rnam par mi rtog pa'i go 'phang bsgrub par bya ba la cung zhig kyang nus pa yod pa ma yin te/_phyin ci log gi zhen pa ni rang dang rjes su mthun pa'i rnam par rtog pa skye ba'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro/_/
[\[54a\]]
[\[54a.1\]]de skad du yang /_shes rab med na mig med pha rol phyin lnga 'di/_/dmigs bu med par byang chub reg par nus ma yin/_/zhes gsungs pa yin no/_/dngos po ma lus pa'i bdag med pa nyid la mngon par zhen pa ni bdag nyid rnam par rtog pa nyid yin na yang phyin
[\[54a.2\]]ci ma log pa'i rang gi yul la zhen pa'i rang bzhin nyid yin pas phyin ci log gi rtog pa ma lus pa dang lhan cig tu 'gal ba yin pa nyid du rtogs te/_gang zhig gang dang dus gcig gi tshe 'gal bar mthong ba de ni shin tu goms pa na yang rang dang 'gal ba shin tu ldog par byed pa ni me las grang
[\[54a.3\]]ba nyid la sogs pa lta bu yin gyi rnam pa gzhan du na phyin ci log gi dogs pas tha snyad thams cad mi 'thad par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/'dir yang /_gal te chos la bdag med so sor rtog_/so sor de rtogs gal te bsgom pa ni/_/de ni mya ngan 'das pa'i 'bras bu'i rgyu/_/rgyu gzhan gang
[\[54a.4\]]yin gyis ni grol mi 'gyur/_/zhes gsungs so/_/bdag med pa la goms pa yang thabs kyi bye brag dang bral ba yin na gang gi phyir des rtog pa'i dri ma ma lus pa dang bral zhing 'gro ba ma lus pa la phan par mdzad pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes skyed par mi nus pa de'i phyir thabs shin tu
[\[54a.5\]]mngon du gyur pa la rab tu 'bad par bya'o/_/skye bo ma lus pa la phan pa'i bdag nyid ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yin la/_phan pa yang mthar thug pa'i rgya che ba las byung ba yin no/_/de'i rgyu yang thabs goms pa kho na yin te/_bdag med pa la goms pa ni rnam par rtog pa tsam spangs
[\[54a.6\]]pa'i 'bras bu can nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/de yang /_zab pa'i phyir dang rgya che'i phyir/_/rnam mi rtog dang yongs su smin/_/'di la de gnyis bstan pas na/_/de phyir bla na med pa'i thabs/_/zhes gsungs so/_/de bas na phyin ci ma log pa'i sbyin pa la sogs pa la sems dpa'i rab tu
[\[54a.7\]]'jug pa ni thabs yin te/_thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la yongs su bsngos par gyur na de dag rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi rgyu nyid du 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/de skad du yang /_sbyin dang tshul khrims bzod dang de bzhin brtson 'grus dang /_/bsam gtan shes rab byang chub yongs su bsngo bar
[\[54b\]]
[\[54b.1\]]gyis/_/byang chub phung por zhen pas mchog 'dzin ma byed ces/_/dang po'i las can de la de skad bstan par bya/_/zhes gsungs pa yin no/_/de ni de lta ma yin te/_rgyu mi 'dra ba goms pa las rdzogs pa'i byang chub goms pa mngon sum du gyur pa dang rjes su mthun pa'i bsgom pa
[\[54b.2\]]med pa'i phyir ro/_/bdag nyid kyi rang gi ngo bo nyid kyis zab pa dang rgya che ba'i bdag nyid can gyi 'bras bu ni rang gi rang bzhin las bsgrub pa'i bya ba yin la/_de'i bdag nyid can gyi rgyu yang 'di la yod pa ma yin te/_sbyin pa la sogs pa'i sems dpa' ni phal cher rang bzhin gyis rgya
[\[54b.3\]]che ba ma yin pa'i yul can yin pa nyid kyi phyir ro/_/smon lam yang dus kyis shin tu bskal pa nyid kyis rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi che ba bdag nyid kyi yul can nyid yin pas rgya che ba ma yin pa'i bdag nyid kyi rnam par rtog pa'i gnyen po ma yin pa nyid do/_/gang gi phyir tha mal pa'i
[\[54b.4\]]rang gi ngo bo skye bo dpag tu med pa la phan pa ma yin pa nyid kyis brtse ba dang ldan pas spang bar bya ba yin no/_/smon lam gyi grogs su gyur pa'i sbyin pa la sogs pa sems dpa'i bdag nyid kyi gnyen po la rab tu 'jug par gyur kyang de'i rgyun yang ldog par mi 'gyur na/_dus gzhan na
[\[54b.5\]]ldog par 'gyur ro zhes gang las yang dag par yid ches par 'gyur/_zab mo la zhen pas rang gi mi mthun pa'i phyogs zad par gyur pa de lta bur gyur pa'i rnam pa ma dmigs pa'i phyir ro/_/rang las bzlog pa gzhan bdag med par bsgoms par gyur pas bdag gi dngos po rtog pa'i
[\[54b.6\]]dri ma med par rab tu sgrub par byed pa ni ma yin te/_de rang gi ngo bo'i rnam par rtog pa dang 'gal bas 'jug pa med pa'i phyir ro/_/gang gi tshe rang gi sems dang tha mi dad pa'i sgo nas 'dzin pa la sogs pa'i rnam pa stong pa nyid du mngon du byed pa de'i tshe de ni bden pa ma yin pa'i rnam par rtog pa ma
[\[54b.7\]]lus pa'i gnyen po nyid du de ltar rtogs par 'gyur ba'i bsgom pa goms par shin tu 'phel bar gyur pas kun du rtog pa ma lus pa bsal ba'i go 'phang bskyed par 'gyur zhes rtog pa yin pa'i phyir rtog pa sngon du gtong ba rnams kyi 'jug pa'i yul du 'gyur ro/_/de bas na rgya che ba ma yin pa'i
[\[55a\]]
[\[55a.1\]]bdag gi dngos por snang ba'i mngon sum gyi gnyen po'i phyogs su gyur pa ma yin pas/_'gro la phan phyir sangs rgyas 'grub par shog_/ces bya ba la sogs pa'i smon lam ni dngos su rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'thob pa'i rgyu ma yin te/_ji skad du/_rigs
[\[55a.2\]]kyi bu khyod de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi de kho na nyid mngon par ma shes par dka' ba spyod pa la spro bas ji ltar bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bar bya snyam zhes gang gsungs pa yin no/_/de bas na bdag med pa dang 'dra bar rgya che ba'i rang gi ngo bo
[\[55a.3\]]yang tha mi dad pa nyid du bsgom par bya'o/_/rgya che ba yang med pa nyid ma yin nam/_bsgom byar bya ba des ji ltar mngon par 'dod pa'i 'bras bu bsgrubs par 'gyur zhe na/_de ni ma yin te/_zad par sa la sogs pa dang 'dra bar yang dag pa ma yin pa bsgom pa goms pa yang gsal por snang
[\[55a.4\]]ba'i rgyu nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/'di ji ltar na yang dag pa ma yin zhe na rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sku'i rnam pa dang bral ba'i rang gi bdag nyid la de'i ngo bo sgro 'dogs pas 'jug pa ni rna ba mos pa yid la byed pa nyid yin pa'i phyir ro zhe na/_de lta na ni de kho na yid la byed pa yang yang dag pa nyid ma
[\[55a.5\]]yin te/_de kho na nyid ji lta ba bzhin yul la 'jug pa ma yin pa'i phyir ro/_/gcig tu rnam par mi rtog pa'i mtshan nyid kyi de kho na nyid la de bzhin du yid la byed pa yang ma yin te/_de ni las dang po pa'i gnas skabs na rnam par rtog pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis 'jug pa yin pa'i phyir ro/_/rnam par
[\[55a.6\]]rtog pa dang bcas pa yin pa de lta na yang dngos po ji lta ba bzhin du gnas pa nyid kyis de kho na nyid ni des nges par byas pa yin pa'i phyir de kho na nyid yid la byed pa nyid du de rnam par gzhag par bya'o/_/de las gzhan pa ni shin tu med pa'i rang gi ngo bo la sgro 'dogs par byed pa yin pa'i phyir mos pa
[\[55a.7\]]yid la byed ces tha snyad gdags pa ste/_tha mal pa'i bdag nyid la thub pa mchog gi rnam pa med bzhin du de kho na nyid dang 'dra bar yid la byed pa'i phyir ro/_/de ni de lta ma yin te/_gang gi phyir bdag med pa yid la byed pas rang gi ngo bo ji lta ba bzhin du gnas pa yul du byed na rang gi yul
[\[55b\]]
[\[55b.1\]]nyid du so sor snang ba'am/_phyin ci log gi rnam par rtog pa'i yul du gyur pa yid la byed ce na/_de la phyogs dang pos ni mos pa yid la byed pa de yang gzhan dang mtshungs pa yin te/_rang gi yul du gyur pa'i rnam pa yongs su 'dzin pa nyid du 'jug pa'i phyir ro/_/rnam pa gzhan du mos pa yid
[\[55b.2\]]la byed pa nyams par thal bar 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/rang gi yul ni rnam par shes pas rtogs par ma gyur pa ni lhag par mos pa'i tha snyad kyi yul ma yin te/_shes pa thams cad rang gi yul du 'dod pa'i rnam par rtog pa'i mtshan nyid can yin pa'i phyir ro/_/de la phyogs gnyis pa de
[\[55b.3\]]yang rigs pa ma yin te/_bdag med pa'i shes pas 'dzin pa la sogs par zhen pas yul du mi byed pa'i phyir ro/_/shes pa las ma gtogs pa gzhan de'i yul can zhes bya ba med pa gang gis na cig shos de yul du byas pa yin no zhes bstan/_de bas na de kho na nyid yid la byed pa dang 'dra
[\[55b.4\]]bar rang gi shes pa'i rnam pa tsam du yul nyid yin pa'i phyir rgya che ba la mos pa yang dag pa ma yin pa ga la yin/_tha mal pa'i bdag nyid 'di ni rgya che ba'i rnam pa la sgro 'dogs pas 'jug pa yang ma yin te/_tha mal pa'i rang gi ngo bo la mos pas rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sku'i rnam pa yul
[\[55b.5\]]du mi byed pa nyid kyi phyir yul ma yin pa la sgro 'dogs pa mi srid pa'i phyir ro/_/tha mal pa'i rang bzhin ni rnam par rtog pa tha mal par snang ba'i mtshan nyid yin la/_bde bar gshegs pa'i rnam pa'i spyod yul yid la byed pa shin tu stobs dang ldan pa ni de'i ngo bor snang ba ma yin no/_/gal te
[\[55b.6\]]yang rgya che ba ma yin pa'i bdag nyid rang gi ngo bo la rnam pa gzhan du cung zhig kyang sgro 'dogs par mi byed na de ji ltar 'di'i gnyen por 'gyur zhe na/_bde bar gshegs pa'i rang gi ngo bor snang ba'i yid la byed pa'i rang gi ngo bo ni tha mal pa ma yin pa'i rang bzhin nyid du skye ba'i phyir dang /_rgyun mi
[\[55b.7\]]'chad par bsgom pa goms pas rigs mthun pa'i shes pa skye ba ni shin tu gsal ba'i rgyu nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/rgya che ba'i shes pa skye ba'i dus de'i tshe cig shos tha mal pa'i rnam pa'i spyod yul shes pas nyams su myong bar 'gyur ba med do/_/tha mal pa'i rang gi ngo bo khong du chud par
[\[56a\]]
[\[56a.1\]]ma gyur pa de yang yod pa nyid du nges par byar mi nus te/_de ni rtog pa tsam nyid kyi rang bzhin nyid yin pa'i phyir ro zhes nges par byas pa yin no/_/de bas na kun du rtog pa spangs pa 'od zer ma lus pa spro ba can gyi kun du bzang po'i bdag nyid sgom par byed pa/_de kho
[\[56a.2\]]na byang chub kyi snod yin te/_de skad du/_phyag rgya'i cho ga gang dag gis/_/bskal pa bye ba grangs med du/_/sangs rgyas nyid ni mi 'thob pa/_/tshe 'di nyid la thob par 'gyur/_/de la bdag tu brtag bya zhing /_/zhes bya ba nas/_rang lha nyid kyi rnal 'byor gyis/_/de phyir bdag nyid
[\[56a.3\]]bsam par bya/_/zhes bya ba'i bar du gsungs pa yin no/_/de ltar yang dag pa yid la byed pa nyid la ltos nas/_bcom ldan 'das ye shes shin tu rdzogs pas de kho na'i rnal 'byor la rdzogs pa'i sgrub pa yang nye bar bsngags pa mdzad de/_rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la mos pa ni
[\[56a.4\]]rdzogs pa'i rnal 'byor dang tha mi dad par mchog tu 'dzin pa'i phyir ro/_/mchog tu 'dzin pa med pa de ni bdag nyid bde bar gshegs pa yid la byed par mi 'gyur te/_bcom ldan 'das ni tha dad par zhen pa spangs pa nyid kyi phyir ro/_/gzhan bcom ldan 'das kyi rnam pa dag la de'i
[\[56a.5\]]mtshan nyid med par rang gi ngo bo la chags pa'i rnam par rtog pa ni kha na ma tho ba med pa'i 'bras bur 'gyur ba yang ma yin te/_de'i phyir rgyal ba'i sku ni mtha' med la/_/yid kyis bdag gzhan mngon zhen dri med lus/_/sangs rgyas kun dang mtshungs par blo gros mchog_/skye bo ma lus re ba'i
[\[56a.6\]]dngos grub 'gyur/_/de la yang thub pa 'od zer dpag tu med pa spro ba dang ldan pa rang dang gzhan gyi phun sum tshogs pa mtha' yas pa'i rten du gyur pa nyid kyis yang dag pa'i thabs kyi mchog gi mtshan nyid can shes rab dang bral bas phongs par 'gyur pa la mngon sum du phyogs pas sgom
[\[56a.7\]]par byed na yang phun sum tshogs pa kun ma lus pa thob par byed pa ma yin pa'i phyir de rang gi ngo bo la phyin ci ma log pa'i sems su bya'o/_/rnyog pa med pa'i phun sum tshogs pa ni shes rab dang thabs las rab tu byung ba nyid kyi phyir ro/_/de dag kyang phyin ci ma log pa'i rgya che ba'i sems dang mtshan nyid gcig
[\[56b\]]
[\[56b.1\]]pa nyid yin na yang tha dad pa'i tha snyad la zhen pas tha dad pa'i phyir ro/_/'di ltar de kho na nyid la sems phyin ci log pa las bzlog pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis shes rab tu shes par bya la/_rang gi 'bras bu la nus pa med pa las bzlog pa ni thabs su bstan pa yin no/_/shes rab yan lag kun
[\[56b.2\]]du 'khyud pa las/_/mchog tu dga' ba nyams su bstar ba yi/_/phun tshogs rang bzhin yan lag thabs gyur te/_/rgyun chad med par blo ldan gyis bsgom bya/_/de'i 'og tu/_shes rab thabs las rab byung ba'i/_/dbyer med dmigs pa'i sprul 'phro bar/_/snang bas yul du
[\[56b.3\]]rnam gzhag pa'i/_/yul gyi rang lus yang dag mchod/_/ji skad bshad pa'i rim pas shes rab dang thabs kyi bdag nyid can gyi rang gi ngo bo mngon du byas nas ji srid sprul pa rnams la des dbang thob par gyur pa de srid du bdag gi ngo bo dang tha mi dad pa'i ngo bo mngon sum du bya ba yin te/_
[\[56b.4\]]phyin ci ma log pa dang rang gi 'bras bu skyed par rung ba nyid kyis na shes rab dang thabs kyi bdag nyid du mtshan nyid gcig pa nyid kyi phyir dang /_rgyud kyang tha mi dad pa'i rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir te/_kun du rtog pa snga ma snga ma las byung ba'i rnam par rtog pa'i rgyun ni rgyud yin te/_sprul pa zhes
[\[56b.5\]]bya ba yang gzhan pa nyid ma yin te/_de bzhin du kun du brtags pa tsam yin pa'i phyir ro/_/kha dog la sogs pa tha dad pas sna tshogs pa'i rang bzhin nyid yin pas ji ltar gcig nyid ces bya zhe na/_de ltar na ni 'ga' zhig kyang gcig nyid du mi 'gyur te/_lha'i sku gcig nyid la yang cha shas
[\[56b.6\]]du ma'i rang bzhin nyid kyis sna tshogs pa'i bdag nyid yin pa'i phyir la/_cha shas med pa yang dmigs par ma gyur pa'i phyir ro/_/ji ltar kun rdzob tu rdzas gcig pa nyid kyis gcig tu rnam par gzhag pa de ltar tshul gzhan pa'i sna tshogs pa'i rang bzhin nyid la yang de'i ngo bor rtogs pa la ltos
[\[56b.7\]]nas thams cad bdag nyid yin no zhes tha mi dad pa'i zhen pas yid la byed pa la 'jug pa'i phyir ro/_/de dag gis ni dngos po thams cad mnyam pa nyid du lhag par mos par bshad pa yin te 'dzin pa la sogs pa'i rnam pa dang bral bar thams cad du mtshungs pa nyid kyi phyir ro/_/gzhan du der_
[\[57a\]]
[\[57a.1\]]snang ba la lhag par zhen pa'i yul rnams las gzhan pa thams cad ces bya ba'i tha snyad kyi gzhir gyur pa gzhan yod pa yang ma yin te/_de rnams kyang cig car rtogs pa'i rang bzhin yin pas tha dad par dbyer mi nus pa'i phyir gcig gi mtshan nyid gzhan yod pa
[\[57a.2\]]yang ma yin no zhes bstan pa yin no/_/de bas na yang dag pa ji lta ba'i rang gi ngo bo so sor rtogs pa la gzhol ba ni kun rdzob 'ba' zhig po 'di la thams cad bdag mtshungs pa yin no zhes shes pa 'jug par 'gyur ba yin gyi dngos po 'ga' la yang gang gis kyang tha dad pa'am/_tha mi dad
[\[57a.3\]]par yul du byed par ni mi nus te/_shes pa thams cad ni rang gi ngo bo tsam la gnas pa nyid kyis gzhan gyi ngo bo yongs su 'dzin pa med la/_yul du ma byas par ni tha dad pa la sogs pa'i tha snyad mi rung ba'i phyir ro/_/de ltar rnal 'byor pa'i rang gi sems rgyu ba re re yang mi mthun pa'i phyogs
[\[57a.4\]]ma lus pa las ldog pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis dkyil 'khor pa'i lha ma lus pa nyid kyi rang bzhin du so sor brtag par bya ba yin te 'di ltar rang rang gi lha'i ting nge 'dzin rnams ni phyin ci log de dang de mi dmigs pas ston par byed pa nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/gang gi phyir sems kyi rang bzhin gang yin pa
[\[57a.5\]]de nyid 'dzin pa la sogs pa'i rnam pa dang bral ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings kyi rang bzhin yin la/_de nyid glo bur gyi dri ma dang bral bas 'od gsal ba nyid yin pa'i phyir dang /_ye shes gzhan bskyed pa'i rgyu mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir me long lta bu'i ye shes kyi bdag nyid yin no/_/mi dmigs pa'i
[\[57a.6\]]snying rje la sogs pa'i bdag nyid kyis rgyud gzhan tha dad par 'dzin pa med pa'i phyir mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes so/_/shes bya thams cad la phyin ci ma log pa'i phyir so sor rtog pa'i ye shes so/_/'gro ba ma lus pa la phan pa'i rgyu yin pa nyid kyis bya ba nan tan gyi ye shes kyi bdag nyid yin no/_/
[\[57a.7\]]de bas na de dag ni go rims bzhin du rtag pa la sogs pa'i bdag po rnams kyi rang bzhin no/_/dmigs pa'i gnyen po nyid kyis rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid dang /_de bzhin du mtshan ma dang log pa'i smon lam dang phyin ci log tu mngon par 'du byed pa'i gnyen po nyid kyis rim
[\[57b\]]
[\[57b.1\]]pa bzhin du/_/mtshan ma med pa dang /_smon pa med pa dang /_mngon par 'du mi byed pa'i rnam par thar pa'i bdag nyid dag yin no/_/de lta bas na go rims bzhin du rdo rje sems ma la sogs pa'i rigs kyi yum gyi rang bzhin te/_stong pa nyid la sogs pa rnam par thar pa'i sgo bzhi po dag
[\[57b.2\]]gis chos kyi dbyings la dmigs par byed pas ting nge 'dzin thams cad skye ba'i rgyu nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/de nyid nang la phyin ci log pa'i gnyen po nyid kyis na nang stong pa nyid kyi rnam pa dang /_phyi dmigs pa med pa'i phyir phyi stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin dang /_de'i rten las mi dmigs pa'i
[\[57b.3\]]rang bzhin nyid kyis phyi nang stong pa nyid kyi bdag nyid can dang /_snod kyi 'jig rten la zhen pa dang bral ba nyid kyis na chen po stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid yin no/_/de'i phyir me long lta bu'i ye shes la brten pa'i rdo rje sems dpa' la sogs pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi rang bzhin yin te/_ming dang gzugs
[\[57b.4\]]la sogs pa'i bag chags yongs su gyur pa me long lta bu'i ye shes ni nang mi dmigs pa la sogs pa'i rten nyid yin pa'i phyir/_ji ltar rang rang gi phyin ci log gi gnyen po nyid kyis/_byang chub kyi sems skye ba dang /_'dren par byed pa dang /_rjes su chags pa dang /_legs so zhes
[\[57b.5\]]bya ba'i rgyu nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/de bzhin du stong pa nyid kyi ye shes kyang mtshan ma med pa'i phyir stong pa nyid stong pa nyid dang /_don dam pa la mchog tu mtshan mar 'dzin par byed pa med pa'i phyir don dam pa stong pa nyid dang /_'dus byas kyis bsod nams nyid kyi tshogs la mtshan mar
[\[57b.6\]]yongs su 'dzin pa med pa'i phyir/_'dus byas stong pa nyid dang /_'dus ma byas byang chub kyi phyogs la yang mtshan mar rjes su 'dzin pa med pa'i phyir 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid yin no/_/de bas na mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes kyi 'khor lo rdo rje rin chen la sogs pa bzhi'i bdag nyid yin
[\[57b.7\]]te/_nyon mongs pa can gyi yid gnas gyur pa'i bdag nyid can mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes 'dzin pa la sogs pa'i sgo nas ji skad du bshad pa'i mtshan mar 'dzin pa med pa'i phyir dang /_rang rang gi mi mthun pa'i phyogs spangs pa'i sgo nas dbang bskur ba dang /_gzi brjid 'phel ba dang /_
[\[58a\]]
[\[58a.1\]]sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la nges par sbyor bar byed pa dang /_rab tu spro bar byed pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro/_/de nyid sems can gyi don la shin tu smon pa'i mngon par zhen pa med pa'i phyir mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid dang /_bdag gis 'khor ba'i
[\[58a.2\]]thog ma dang tha ma med pa yongs su dor bar bya'o zhes smon pa len pa med pa'i phyir thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid dang /_bdag gi phung po lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings la yang dge ba yongs su dor bar mi bya'o zhes mngon par zhen pa med pa'i phyir dor ba med pa stong
[\[58a.3\]]pa nyid dang /_bdag gis rang gi mtshan nyid kyi rigs ni yongs su sbyong bar bya'o zhes don du gnyer ba dang bral ba'i phyir rang bzhin stong pa nyid yin no/_/de'i phyir rnam par rtog pa'i yid gnas gyur pa'i mtshan nyid can so sor rtog pa'i ye shes la brten pa rdo rje chos la sogs pa bzhi po'i
[\[58a.4\]]bdag nyid yin te/_rnam par rtog pa'i yid gnas gyur pa'i mtshan nyid can gyi so sor rtog pa'i ye shes ni ji skad du bshad pa'i phyin ci log gis dben pas chos kyi de kho na nyid so sor rtog pa nyid yin pa'i phyir dang /_de'i sgo nas kyang rang bzhin gyis dag pa'i chos nyid dang shes rab dang /_ye
[\[58a.5\]]shes las phyir mi ldog pa nyid dang /_dgongs pa'i don ma lus pa yongs su shes pa'i rgyu nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/de nyid mtshan dang dpe byad kyi bdag nyid can gyi gzugs kyi sku la mngon par zhen pa med pa'i phyir rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid dang /_stobs dang /_mi 'jigs pa la
[\[58a.6\]]sogs pa'i rang bzhin gyi chos kyi sku la mngon par zhen pa med pa'i phyir/_/chos thams cad stong pa nyid dang /_gang zag dang chos su kun nas sgro 'dogs pa med pa'i phyir dngos po med pa stong pa nyid dang /_ji skad du bshad pa'i stong pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid la skur pa mi 'debs pa dang /_
[\[58a.7\]]mngon par zhen pa med pa'i phyir dngos po med pa'i rang bzhin stong pa nyid yin no/_/de bas na bya ba nan tan gyi ye shes la brten pa rdo rje chos la sogs pa bzhi po'i bdag nyid yin te/_mig la sogs pa'i shes pa gnas gyur pa'i bdag nyid bya ba nan tan gyi ye shes ni ji skad du bshad
[\[58b\]]
[\[58b.1\]]pa'i phyin ci log spangs pa'i sgo nas bde bar gshegs pa ma lus pa mchod pa dang /_kun nas bsrung ba dang /_bgegs bsal ba dang /_lus la sogs pa stong pa nyid kyi ye shes kyi rgyu nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/de bzhin du ser sna dang /_'chal ba'i tshul khrims dang mi bzod pa dang /_
[\[58b.2\]]le lo dag gi gnyen po nyid kyis de nyid sbyin pa dang /_tshul khrims dang /_bzod pa dang /_brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bdag nyid yin no/_/de'i phyir gsang ba'i mchod pa bzhi po'i rang bzhin yin te/_go rims bzhin du me long lta bu'i ye shes la sogs pa bsgrub
[\[58b.3\]]pa ni rang gi rnam par thar pa'i sgo rnam par dag pa'i stobs kyi lhun gyis grub par mngon par 'dod pa'i khyad par skyed par byed pa nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/_/de nyid rnam par g.yeng ba dang /_shes rab 'chal pa dang /_yang dag pa ma yin pa'i smon lam dang /_thabs ma yin pa

[\[63a.1\]]de nas ser sna can dang dbul po rnams la dmigs/_spro bsdu ci nus bya ste yid skyo na sngags bzlas so/_/de nas yi ge brgya pa brjod la/_dge ba ji ltar 'dod par bsngos la btang ngo /_/langs la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ci rigs par klag go/_/

[\[67b\]]
[\[67b.1\]]du cung zad 'dud par byas pa ni bud med kyi sgyu 'phrul lo/_/snying gar rdo rje bsdams pa 'byed pa ni rdo rje dral ba'o/_/rdo rje khu tshur gyi mthe'u chung gnyis bsgreng ste bzlog la kha'i 'gram du mche ba'i tshul du bzhag pa ni rdo rje mche ba'o/_/g.yon pa'i khu tshur gyi shubs nas drangs te g.yas
[\[67b.2\]]pa'i khu tshur gyis dpung mgor ral gri 'dzin pa'i tshul du bzhag pa ni ral gri'i thabs so/_/g.yon pa'i mdzub mo dang g.yas pa'i mthe'u chung mdud par byas te g.yas pa'i mdzub mo lcags kyu ltar byas pas 'gugs pa ni lcags kyu'i thabs so/_/rdo rje khu tshur gnyis kyis g.yon
[\[67b.3\]]du 'debs pa ltar byed pa ni mdung thung gi thabs so/_/lag pa g.yon dkur brten pa la g.yas pa'i khu tshur gyis thag mdung bskor ba'i tshul du lan gsum du bskor nas 'phen pa ni thag mdung 'phen pa'i thabs so/_/rdo rje bsnun pa'i tshul ni rdo rje'i stang stabs so/_/lag pa gnyis

[\[67b.5\]]rnams rdung ba ltar byed pa ni gtun shing gi thabs so/_/g.yon pa'i rdo rje khu tshur snying gar bstan par byas la g.yas pa'i rdo rje khu tshur las gung mo brkyang ba'i tshigs dang por mdzub mo bkug nas dpung mgor bzhag pa ni ba dan gyi thabs so/_/g.yon pa dkur brten la g.yas pas
[\[67b.6\]]snying ga nas 'gugs pa'i tshul du byed pa'i snying ga de nyid du rdo rje sems dpa' ltar 'jog pa ni rdo rje 'gugs byed do/_/snying ga'i mdun du 'gying bag dang bcas pas lag pa yongs su bskor ba ni rdo rje 'jo tshul lo/_/g.yon pa dkur brtan la g.yas pa mi 'jigs pa'i tshul du byed pa ni

[\[68a.1\]]bstod pa'i tshul du snying gar bzhag pa ni phyag 'tshal ba'i tshul lo/_/g.yon pa dkur brten la g.yas pa rdo rje rtse gsum pa 'phen pa'i tshul du byed pa ni rdo rje 'phen pa'o/_/kha'i steng 'og tu lag pa gnyis bkan te de nyid dang 'jigs su rung ba ltar
